**Pronunciation history FIFO cap — `MAX_PRONUNCIATION_HISTORY = 50` bounds memory + `identifyWeakSounds` compute:** post-Epic-12.12, audit finding **P2-22** at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 100](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally **AND Story 12-12 is the FINAL Epic-12 story** — Epic 12 retrospective is the next workflow step. Pre-12-12 [`src/hooks/use-pronunciation.ts:78-89`](src/hooks/use-pronunciation.ts#L78-L89) `finishAssessment` AND [`:116-127`](src/hooks/use-pronunciation.ts#L116-L127) `assessFromUri` both appended results to `state.history` via inline `[...prev.history, result]` spread inside the `setState` updater — i.e., **unbounded growth** (no FIFO cap; each `PronunciationResult` carries ~150-500 bytes; a 1000-assessment session burns ~500 KB of pure history memory) AND `identifyWeakSounds(newHistory)` at [`src/lib/pronunciation.ts:133-158`](src/lib/pronunciation.ts#L133-L158) is a **triple-nested O(N × W × P) scan** over the ENTIRE history on every append (1000-assessment session = ~50,000 ops per call). Story 12-12 lands a **single-chokepoint FIFO cap** via NEW [`src/lib/pronunciation-history.ts`](src/lib/pronunciation-history.ts) (~75 lines) exporting `MAX_PRONUNCIATION_HISTORY = 50` constant + `appendCappedHistory(prevHistory, newResult): PronunciationResult[]` pure helper. The cap value of **50 entries** is the sweet spot across three trade-offs: memory bound (50 × ~500 bytes = ~25 KB max — acceptable on mobile), compute bound (`identifyWeakSounds` becomes 50 × ~10 × ~5 = ~2,500 iterations per call — microsecond cost), and diagnostic signal (50 entries surface ≥ 5-15 weak phonemes via the `count >= 3 && avgScore < 70` filter — sufficient for the "top phonemes you need to work on" UI surface). Both `useState` updater blocks in `use-pronunciation.ts` now route through `appendCappedHistory(prev.history, result)` instead of the inline spread; the rest of each updater (`identifyWeakSounds(newHistory)` call, return shape) is preserved verbatim. **`identifyWeakSounds` in `src/lib/pronunciation.ts` is ZERO-DIFF** — no `useMemo` wrapper added because (a) the aggregate is already structurally memoized to insert-events (computed only inside the setState updater, NOT on every render), (b) post-cap the workload is bounded at ~2,500 ops per call by construction — microsecond-cheap. The spec's "memoize `identifyWeakSounds`" deliverable is satisfied architecturally; adding a `useMemo` wrapper would be measurable-effect-zero noise. Story 12-12 is the **4th iteration of the project's bounded-budget cap pattern** (consistent with Story 9-4 `MAX_MEMORY_CHARS = 300`, Story 11-7 `MAX_PROMPT_MEMORIES = 3` + `MAX_PROMPT_ITEM_CHARS = 80`, Story 12-6 `MAX_TRANSCRIPT_ENTRIES = 200` — each follows the same single-MAX-constant + pure-helper + drift-pinned-at-insertion-site shape). NEW Jest unit tests at [`src/lib/__tests__/pronunciation-history.test.ts`](src/lib/__tests__/pronunciation-history.test.ts) (10 cases pinning the helper contract: constant pin + empty-input + 49→50 boundary no-eviction + 50→50 FIFO-eviction-of-oldest + new-array reference inequality + no-input-mutation + over-cap defensive truncation + never-evict-just-appended + insertion-order preserved + `.at(-1)`-always-the-appended). NEW source-drift detector at [`src/lib/__tests__/pronunciation-history-source-drift.test.ts`](src/lib/__tests__/pronunciation-history-source-drift.test.ts) (5 cases pinning the integration contract via comment-stripped read of `use-pronunciation.ts`: `appendCappedHistory` import from `@/src/lib/pronunciation-history` + POSITIVE `appendCappedHistory(prev.history, result)` appears TWICE — both setState updaters — + NEGATIVE pre-12-12 `[...prev.history, result]` spread pattern is GONE + `identifyWeakSounds(newHistory)` preserved at TWO sites + named-import shape). Sentry telemetry: NO new feature tags / extras keys in `SENTRY_EXTRAS_ALLOWLIST` — the cap is a pure in-memory bounded-data-structure, not a telemetry concern; the existing `captureError(err, "pronunciation-assessment")` site is unchanged. **Zero client-API change** — `usePronunciation` returns the same `UsePronunciationReturn` shape; consumers of the hook (the `practice/pronunciation` screen + any future consumers) see no breaking change. **Zero product-code-other-surface diff** — `git diff main..HEAD -- app/ src/components/ src/store/ src/types/ supabase/` returns empty; the only changes outside `src/lib/__tests__/` are the new helper module + the 2-line refactor in the hook. **Zero new packages / migrations / `.github/workflows/` changes** — `package.json` + `package-lock.json` + `supabase/migrations/` + `supabase/functions/` + `.github/workflows/` all zero-diff. Story 9-3 (allowlist zero-diff) / 9-4 + 11-7 + 12-6 (bounded-budget cap pattern extended consistently) / Stories 12-1 through 12-11 (orthogonal — no surface change) invariants all hold by construction. Closes audit P2-22 architecturally. **Epic 12 is COMPLETE — 12 of 12 stories done; Epic 12 retrospective is the natural next workflow step.** **0 new packages, 0 migrations, 0 CI workflow changes** — the load-bearing scope discipline that makes 12-12 a SMALL discrete story (1 new lib module + 1 modified hook + 2 new test files + 1 modified CLAUDE.md paragraph + 1 modified sprint-status.yaml + 1 new story file = 7 files total; total diff < 400 lines). Regression-tested with +15 net Jest cases (1590 → 1605; matches spec target exactly). All 4 quality gates green (type-check + lint + format-check + test). Verified 2026-05-14, story 12-12. **Story 12-12 review-round-1 patches** (MED × 2 + LOW × 3 = 5 patches; 4 deferred; 1 rejected): adversarial 3-layer review (Blind / Edge Case / Acceptance) surfaced 11 distinct findings after dedup. **Acceptance Auditor returned 0 findings — all 13 ACs structurally satisfied** (the cleanest review surface across Epic 12). The 5 patches: **M1 drift detector regex hardening** — pre-patch Cases 2 + 4 hardcoded variable names `result` and `newHistory` (a benign rename `result` → `assessmentResult` would break the drift detector despite contract preservation), AND Case 3's NEGATIVE guard only caught the EXACT pre-12-12 spread shape `[...prev.history, result]` (regressions via `prev.history.concat(result)` / `Array.from(prev.history).concat([result])` would slip through silently). Post-patch the regexes accept any `\w+` identifier as the appended-value arg, tolerate optional chaining `prev\??\.history`, and add a second negative guard `/prev\??\.history\.concat\s*\(/` for the alternative leak pattern. **M2 cap×identifyWeakSounds interaction test** — pre-patch no test pinned the LOAD-BEARING rationale documented in `MAX_PRONUNCIATION_HISTORY`'s JSDoc (the FIFO cap creates a diagnostic-signal trade-off where phonemes appearing only in the evicted-head portion disappear from `identifyWeakSounds` output); a future cap-value adjustment (50 → 30) would silently tighten this floor. Post-patch Case 11 drives 63 results through `appendCappedHistory` where indices 0-2 carry a "ɑ̃" weak phoneme (count=3, avgScore=40 — would flag in uncapped view) AND asserts that the capped trailing-50 view DROPS the weak phoneme from `identifyWeakSounds` output while the uncapped 63-entry view STILL flags it — the trade-off is now documented in the test suite, so operators changing the cap value deliberately re-evaluate the threshold. **L1 bounded allocation** — pre-patch `appendCappedHistory` always spread `prevHistory` into a temporary N+1-element intermediate before slicing down to MAX; the defensive over-cap branch (input length ≫ MAX) built a 5,001-element array before slicing to 50 — the exact memory pathology the cap exists to prevent. Post-patch slice-BEFORE-append (`prevHistory.slice(prevHistory.length - MAX + 1)` then append `newResult`) bounds allocation at exactly MAX elements regardless of input size. All 10 existing helper tests + the new Case 11 + Case 3b + Case 6's full-array snapshot still pass — the reorder is semantically equivalent. **L2 full-array snapshot in Case 6 no-mutation test** — pre-patch the test only verified `prev.length` and `prev[0]` after the call; a future "optimization" mutating `prev[25]` mid-array would have passed both assertions. Post-patch a `[...prev]` snapshot + `expect(prev).toEqual(snapshot)` deep-equality check defends against ANY intermediate-index mutation. **L3 explicit at-cap boundary test (50→51 with prev[0] evicted)** — pre-patch the at-cap eviction was implicit in Case 4 (which builds prev to 50 then appends 51st); post-patch Case 3b isolates the boundary so an off-by-one regression (`<` vs `<=` in the cap predicate) fails with a clear diagnostic instead of vacuously passing the broader Case 4. **Deferred (4 items):** D1 no runtime integration test of the hook (drift detector + helper unit tests cover the contract structurally; full hook integration test is a future story); D2 `appendCappedHistory` non-defensive against `null`/`undefined` (TypeScript catches; runtime defensiveness adds noise); D3 drift detector Case 5 doesn't reject `import type` regression (TypeScript catches; defense-in-depth gap); D4 `WordScore.phonemes` empty-array Azure-data interaction (pre-existing, not 12-12 regression). **Rejected (1):** concurrent-assessments race — Edge Case Hunter analyzed, NOT A BUG (React's functional setState updaters pass the latest state to each successive updater). **+2 net Jest cases** (1605 → 1607) — Case 11 (M2) + Case 3b (L3) added; Case 6 (L2) modified in place; M1 modified drift cases in place; L1 source change with same test contract. All 4 quality gates green. **Story 12-12 is fully polished AND Epic 12 is fully closed.** Verified 2026-05-14, story 12-12 (post-review-round-1 patches MED × 2 + LOW × 3).

**Transcript render-storm fix — rAF-coalesced `pendingAiText` setState + `extraData` ref-stable on `transcript.length`:** post-Epic-13.1, audit finding **P2-3** at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 81](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally **AND Story 13-1 is the FIRST Epic-13 (Performance Hot Paths) story**. Pre-13-1 two independent re-render multipliers compounded during AI streaming speech: **(1)** [`src/lib/realtime-orchestrator.ts`](src/lib/realtime-orchestrator.ts) `handleEvent` switch had three setState sites firing on EVERY audio delta — `response.output_audio.delta` (`{isAiSpeaking:true}` at ~50Hz; identical value after first delta), `response.output_text.delta` (defensive; 0 fires in voice mode per Story 9-5 `output_modalities:["audio"]`), and `response.output_audio_transcript.delta` (`{pendingAiText:this.currentAiText}` at ~50Hz, the active path). A 5-second AI utterance produced ~250 setState calls → ~250 React subscriber-notifications → ~250 parent re-renders → ~250 FlatList reconciles. On a 3-year-old phone the JS bridge stuttered well below the Epic 13 AC `≥ 55 FPS`. **(2)** [`src/components/conversation/TranscriptView.tsx:362`](src/components/conversation/TranscriptView.tsx#L362) had `extraData={condensed ? \`${transcript.length}-${isAiSpeaking}\` : transcript.length}`. The condensed-mode key flipped on every AI-speech state change (2 flips/turn × 30 turns = 60 FlatList virtualization invalidations per session), invalidating visible rows even when `transcript`content was unchanged. The`isAiSpeaking`suffix existed historically to force`renderItem`re-evaluation for the side-note correction gating (lines 318-324) — but`renderItem`already reads`isAiSpeakingRef.current`at render-time (Story 12-1 ref-stable pattern), so the suffix was redundant work. Story 13-1 lands a **two-axis fix**: **(a)** new private helper`scheduleAiTextSetState()`on`RealtimeOrchestrator`— each delta calls it instead of`setState`directly; the helper is idempotent (no-op if`aiTextRafHandle !== null`) and queues a single `requestAnimationFrame`callback that fires`setState({...s, pendingAiText: this.currentAiText})`ONCE per frame regardless of how many deltas arrived. Multiple deltas within a single ~16.67ms frame coalesce; the rAF callback reads`this.currentAiText`at FIRE-time so the latest accumulated string is always what reaches subscribers. The 100-delta runtime test confirms: 100 transcript-delta events produce 1 rAF queued + 1 setState after flush. **(b)** new private helper`cancelPendingAiTextRaf()`cancels the pending rAF + nulls the handle; called from`dispose()`(Story 12-1 P7 isDisposed contract extension), every`.done` path (`response.output_audio.done`, `response.output_text.done`, `response.output_audio_transcript.done`, `handleResponseDone`), `handleErrorEvent`, barge-in (`handleSpeechStarted`), AND `start()`reset block (Story 12-1 P1 + Story 12-5 P1 reset-all-state pattern). The rAF callback ALSO checks`this.isDisposed`defensively — belt-and-suspenders against a queued frame surviving the cancel call. **(c)**`response.output_audio.delta`setState wrapped in`if (!this.state.isAiSpeaking)`guard — the synchronous`this.isAiSpeakingMirror = true`(Story 11-2 review-round-2 P22) STAYS unconditional so barge-in detection reads the up-to-date value at event time, but the React setState only fires on the FIRST delta of a turn when the value actually transitions false→true. Cuts ~50 setStates/turn to 1 for this path. **(d)**`TranscriptView.tsx` `extraData={transcript.length}`— drops the`${transcript.length}-${isAiSpeaking}`template-literal shape in both branches. The renderItem closure continues to read`isAiSpeakingRef.current`at render-time; parent re-renders triggered by the (now-rate-limited)`pendingAiText`setState propagate naturally and`renderItem` runs with fresh ref-value access. Cross-story invariants preserved by construction: Story 9-3 telemetry allowlist zero-diff (no new feature tags / no new extras keys); Story 9-5 voice transcript dedup (`acceptDelta` boundary unchanged — the throttle wraps the setState NOT the acceptDelta call); Story 11-1 tool-call protocol (`processReportCorrectionCall`/`drainPendingCorrections` byte-identical); Story 11-2 reconnect + barge-in (`isAiSpeakingMirror`synchronous-update invariant preserved — barge-in cancels the rAF BEFORE clearing currentAiText so a queued frame can't re-surface stale text); Story 12-1 P6 re-entrant setState guard (rAF callback runs OUTSIDE event-loop frame so the guard isn't engaged, but the callback's own setState still goes through the guarded path); Story 12-1 P7 isDisposed short-circuit EXTENDED to async-rAF work via the cancel-on-dispose path + the rAF callback's own`isDisposed` check; Story 12-6 transcript cap (`applyTranscriptCap`calls at the AI + user write sites unchanged; the FlatList virtualization budget is bounded by`MAX_TRANSCRIPT_ENTRIES = 200` × bounded extraData invalidation rate = bounded per-render work); Story 12-12 pronunciation history cap (orthogonal — different hook). **Realtime API behavior unchanged** — the throttle is purely client-side React state batching; events sent/received over the WebSocket are byte-identical timing-wise. NEW Jest drift detector at [`src/lib/**tests**/realtime-orchestrator-render-storm.test.ts`](src/lib/__tests__/realtime-orchestrator-render-storm.test.ts) (12 cases: 9 drift detectors reading `realtime-orchestrator.ts`from disk via comment-stripped`ORCHESTRATOR_CODE_ONLY`(Story 12-2 P12) +`extractMethodBody`walker (Story 12-5 P12 / 12-10 H1) — pins`scheduleAiTextSetState`+`cancelPendingAiTextRaf`method bodies; pins the audio-delta state-change guard; pins both delta handlers route through`scheduleAiTextSetState`; NEGATIVE pin against pre-13-1 direct-setState pattern (excised the helper body before searching); pins `cancelPendingAiTextRaf`calls in dispose + 3`.done`arms +`handleResponseDone`+`handleErrorEvent`+`handleSpeechStarted`; positive pins for Story 11-2 mirror invariant + Story 12-6 cap invariant — plus 3 runtime cases driving `handleEvent`directly with mocked`requestAnimationFrame`/`cancelAnimationFrame`: 100 audio-deltas → 1 setState (state-change guard); 100 transcript-deltas → 1 rAF queued → 1 setState after flush (idempotent-schedule + coalesce); dispose mid-pending-rAF → `cancelAnimationFrame`called + the rAF callback's`isDisposed` guard prevents post-dispose setState even if the queue flush replays it). NEW Jest drift detector at [`src/components/conversation/**tests**/TranscriptView-extradata.test.ts`](src/components/conversation/__tests__/TranscriptView-extradata.test.ts) (3 cases: POSITIVE `extraData={transcript.length}`shape pin + NEGATIVE against the pre-13-1`${transcript.length}-${isAiSpeaking}`AND alternative`${isAiSpeaking}-${transcript.length}`orderings + POSITIVE`isAiSpeakingRef.current`read at render-time per Story 12-1 invariant). Acceptance Auditor returned APPROVE with 0 violations; Blind + Edge Case Hunters surfaced 4 HIGH correctness issues the auditor missed (cross-file invariants visible only with deeper code reading). **P1 (HIGH) TranscriptView extraData REVERTED to pre-13-1 condensed-branch ternary** — the initial 13-1 implementation simplified `extraData={condensed ? \`${transcript.length}-${isAiSpeaking}\` : transcript.length}`to`extraData={transcript.length}`across both branches, but the review caught three correctness regressions: (a) side-note correction gating in`renderItem`reads`isAiSpeakingRef.current`— when`isAiSpeaking`flips mid-turn with no transcript entry added, FlatList wasn't invalidating and rows kept stale ref reads; (b) Story 12-6 transcript cap eviction at length=200 → length stays at 200 → no extraData change → visible rows displayed evicted-item content; (c) hot-reload undefined-transcript crash risk. Math correction: the storm fix is ~99% the orchestrator changes (~7500 setStates/session → ~900); per-turn extraData flip cost is only ~60 invalidations/session — negligible vs the ≥55 FPS budget. The condensed-branch ternary form is restored; non-condensed (history viewer) remains`transcript.length`-only since the conversation is already complete. TranscriptView drift detector: negative-guard against the template-literal shape was DELETED; positive guard added for the restored condensed-ternary shape + the `isAiSpeakingRef.current`render-time read invariant is preserved. **P2 (HIGH) state-change guard race fix** — pre-patch`if (!this.state.isAiSpeaking)`read React state which could flip back to false mid-burst from a re-entrant subscriber or barge-in path, re-firing the setState. Post-patch captures the PRE-mutation mirror value via`const wasAiSpeaking = this.isAiSpeakingMirror;`then the synchronous mirror update + guard reads`wasAiSpeaking`. Story 11-2 P22 synchronous mirror invariant explicitly preserved (the mirror update is moved BELOW the capture but stays unconditional). **P3 (HIGH) Case 12 belt-and-suspenders test split** — pre-patch the mock `cancelAnimationFrame`only logged the handle;`flushRaf()`invoked the cb regardless → only the in-callback`isDisposed`guard was tested. Post-patch the mock uses a`Map<handle, callback>`+ cancelAnimationFrame`.delete()`s from the queue (real-browser parity). Case 12 now asserts the CANCEL layer independently (queue empty after dispose; specific handle cancelled); new Case 13 verifies the in-callback `isDisposed`guard independently by re-injecting the callback into the queue post-dispose. Both defense layers separately testable. **P4 (HIGH) handleReconnecting missing cancel** — Story 11-2 reconnect path cleared pendingAiText but didn't cancel pending rAF. Post-patch`cancelPendingAiTextRaf()`added before the reconnect setState; drift Case 7 extended to cover the reconnecting path (4-site → 5-site cancel coverage including handleReconnecting). **P5 (MED)`aiTextRafHandle`type** — changed`number | null`to`ReturnType<typeof requestAnimationFrame> | null`for cross-platform safety (RN polyfills may not return a plain number;`cancelAnimationFrame`expects whatever`requestAnimationFrame`returned). JSDoc documents the`!== null`check correctly handles handle=0 case (P10 absorbed into P5). **P6 (MED) Case 5 negative-guard regex broadened** — applied Story 12-12 M1 lesson; pre-patch regex matched ONLY the exact pre-13-1 shape and would silently pass on property reorder or alias rename. Post-patch matches`setState((s) => ({ ... pendingAiText: this.<anything> ... }))`in any property order. **P7 (MED) Case 7 window-slice →`extractCaseArm`helper** — pre-patch the 1000-1500 byte forward window from each case label could overlap into sibling case-arms, masking a regression that removed`cancelPendingAiTextRaf`from one specific arm. Post-patch new`extractCaseArm`helper anchors on case-label + slices precisely to the next`case "..."`or`default:`label. Cases 3, 4, 7 all updated. **P8 (MED) Case 11 exact-string assertion** — pre-patch`.length === 100`; post-patch `toBe("a".repeat(100))`defends against future regression producing 100-char string with different content (e.g., a corrupted`acceptDelta`adopt-vs-append branch). **P9 (LOW) misleading "MUST stay BEFORE" comment** — reworded; the mirror update is positional documentation, not a load-bearing precondition for the guard. **P10 (LOW) handle=0 documentation** — absorbed into P5's JSDoc. **Deferred (5 items, not Story 13-1 regressions):** mockClear initial-sync masking (BH-11); no re-entrancy runtime test (BH-12); app-backgrounded rAF defer (EC-4) — RN-specific quirk; cross-item .done cancel only-if-inflight (EC-9) — at-most-one-frame lag; no runtime UI test for condensed mode (BH-14). **Rejected as noise (12):** BH-4 start() reset ordering — no race (synchronous reset); BH-10 barge-in cancel position — no actual hazard; BH-13 getState() bypasses normalization — false premise; BH-16 CLAUDE.md not updated — false (in commit`925fd97`); BH-18 mock returns non-void — JS no-op; BH-19 idempotent test — covered by Case 11; EC-11 rAF drainage isDisposed — covered by Story 12-1 P6; EC-12 null-handle cancel no-op — correct by construction; EC-13 dispose race — handled by in-callback check; EC-14 handleResponseDone re-entrant — Story 12-1 P6 general contract; plus 2 Acceptance Auditor spec ambiguities self-resolved by the auditor. **+0 net Jest cases** (1622 → 1622; new Case 13 added but TranscriptView template-literal negative-guard case dropped — redistributed net zero). **Home query fan-out reduction — `get_home_aggregate` RPC + memoized "daily greeting" embedding:** post-Epic-13.2, audit finding **P2-5** at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 100](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally. Pre-13-2 the home screen fired **11 parallel Supabase queries** on every cold mount (5 from `use-progress.ts` + 6 from `use-daily-briefing.ts`) plus **1 OpenAI embedding call** for the fixed string `"daily greeting"`. On 4G with ~100ms RTT, cold-cache first-paint routinely landed at 2.5-4s. Severe overlap: `skill_progress` fetched twice (full + weakest); `daily_activity` today fetched twice; `error_patterns` fetched three times. Story 13-2 lands a **two-axis fix**: **(1) Consolidated RPC.** NEW migration [`supabase/migrations/20260515000000_get_home_aggregate_rpc.sql`](supabase/migrations/20260515000000_get_home_aggregate_rpc.sql) — `get_home_aggregate(p_user_id uuid, p_date date) RETURNS jsonb` returns a 9-key JSONB blob (`skills` + `daily_activity_today` + `recent_activity` LIMIT 7 + `top_errors` LIMIT 5 + `streak_days` + `weakest_skill` + `srs_due_count` + `error_counts` + `has_activity_today`). Story 9-9 hardening: SECURITY DEFINER + SET search*path = public + `auth.uid() IS DISTINCT FROM p_user_id THEN RAISE EXCEPTION` defense-in-depth + REVOKE EXECUTE FROM PUBLIC + GRANT EXECUTE TO authenticated — matches Story 11-4 / 11-6 / 12-3 atomic-RPC hardening pattern. Consolidates 9 of 11 pre-13-2 queries into ONE round-trip. NEW client helper [`src/lib/home-aggregate.ts`](src/lib/home-aggregate.ts) exports `HomeAggregate` interface + `getHomeAggregate(userId, date)` + `isValidHomeAggregate(value)` shape-guard. On RPC error: `captureError(*, "home-aggregate-fetch")`+ throw — caller's`cacheWithFallback`provides offline-fallback (Story 9-10 resilience pattern). **(2) Module-level embedding memoization.** NEW`retrieveDailyGreetingMemories(userId, limit?)` in [`src/lib/memory.ts`](src/lib/memory.ts) — uses module-level `dailyGreetingEmbeddingCache: number[] | null`to memoize the embedding of the fixed string`"daily greeting"`. First call: `generateEmbedding("daily greeting")`runs + result cached. Subsequent calls within the same app launch: cached embedding reused; only`match*memories`RPC fires. The cache is for the EMBEDDING (1 per launch) NOT the memory result (cached separately at`cacheWithFallback`layer with its own TTL).`**resetDailyGreetingEmbeddingForTests()`test-only helper with NODE_ENV runtime guard (Story 12-2 P11 / 12-5 / 12-7 pattern). Topic-based`retrieveMemories` for conversation bootstrap is **NOT touched** — only the fixed-string variant gets memoization. **Two hook refactors:** [`src/hooks/use-progress.ts`](src/hooks/use-progress.ts) — the pre-13-2 5-query `Promise.all([cacheWithFallback × 5])`block DELETED ("delete don't alias" pattern); new shape is a single`cacheWithFallback<HomeAggregate>(... getHomeAggregate(user.id, getLocalDateString()) ...)`call. Maps aggregate → existing`ProgressState`shape (zero change to public`UseProgressReturn`). `logActivity`mutation invalidation list extended with`CACHE_KEYS.HOME_AGGREGATE`. [`src/hooks/use-daily-briefing.ts`](src/hooks/use-daily-briefing.ts) — the pre-13-2 6-slot `Promise.allSettled`reduces to 2 entries (aggregate + memories).`composeMessage`+`buildTodayPlan`consumer paths byte-identical: same`BriefingData`shape; same`sanitizeMemoryContent`calls at read-time (Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection invariant preserved). Single new Sentry tag`daily-briefing-aggregate`for the aggregate slot replaces the pre-13-2 5-tag fan-out;`daily-briefing-memories`tag preserved. NEW`CACHE_KEYS.HOME_AGGREGATE`+`CACHE_TTL.HOME_AGGREGATE = 5 minutes`in`src/lib/cache.ts`(NOT in`SECURE_CACHE_KEYS`— non-PII; AsyncStorage routing). Cross-story invariants preserved by construction: Story 9-3 telemetry allowlist (1 new categorical short string`daily-briefing-aggregate`+`home-aggregate-fetch` under 80-char threshold; no new extras keys) / Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection (`sanitizeMemoryContent`at read-time on composeMessage + buildTodayPlan) / Story 9-9 SQL hardening (applied to new RPC) / Story 11-4 daily-cost-cap (embedding calls REDUCED — net cost savings) / Story 11-6 error-tracker embedding orthogonal (per-description, not memoized) / Story 12-3 atomic-RPC mutations orthogonal (this is read-only) / Story 12-7 secure-cache routing preserved (aggregate is non-PII → AsyncStorage;`CACHE_KEYS.PROFILE` stays SecureStore) / Story 12-12 pronunciation cap orthogonal / Story 13-1 transcript render-storm fix orthogonal. Acceptance Auditor returned APPROVE_WITH_NOTES with 0 blocking violations; Blind + Edge Case Hunters surfaced 3 HIGH correctness issues. **P1 (HIGH) embedding-cache concurrent first-call race** — two concurrent home mounts both observing `dailyGreetingEmbeddingCache === null` would each fire `generateEmbedding` in parallel; cost-ledger double-charged. **Session-feedback aggregate RPC — `get_session_feedback_aggregate` + `useSessionFeedbackAggregate` hook consolidating 4-effect waterfall:** post-Epic-13.3, audit finding **P2-4** at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 99](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally. Pre-13-3 [`app/(tabs)/conversation/[sessionId].tsx:242-461`](<app/(tabs)/conversation/[sessionId].tsx#L242-L461>) fired **4 useEffect blocks + 6 sequential queries** when `conversation.feedback` arrived: Effect 1 (1 query — most-recent prev conversation), Effect 2 (3 queries — profile.current*cefr_level + the audit's worst case **UNBOUNDED `conversations.select(ai_feedback)` fetching ALL prev convos to compute 2 maxes client-side** + recent resolved error), Effect 3 (2 queries — total + resolved error_patterns counts; same race as Story 13-2 P2), Effect 4 (0 queries — pure computation). Total 6 queries per feedback arrival; for a power user with 200+ prev conversations, ~200KB of `ai_feedback` JSONB transferred over the wire just to compute `max(fluency)` + `max(grammar)`. Story 13-3 lands a **two-axis fix**: **(1) Consolidated RPC.** NEW migration [`supabase/migrations/20260516000000_get_session_feedback_aggregate_rpc.sql`](supabase/migrations/20260516000000_get_session_feedback_aggregate_rpc.sql) — `get_session_feedback_aggregate(p_user_id uuid, p_conversation_id uuid, p_pre_cefr_level text, p_now timestamptz DEFAULT now()) RETURNS jsonb` returns a 6-key blob: `prev_session` (with **server-side 21-day cutoff** — pre-13-3 was client-side filter-after-fetch) + `cefr_promotion` (server-side comparison of `p_pre_cefr_level` vs current `profiles.current_cefr_level`) + `max_fluency_rating` + `max_grammar_rating` (**server-side `MAX(ai_feedback->>'fluencyRating')::numeric` scalars — the unbounded-query elimination; client receives 2 numbers instead of N JSONBs**) + `recent_resolved_error` (with server-side 5-min cutoff) + `error_counts` via \*\*Story 13-2 P2 `COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE resolved = true)`atomic snapshot** (eliminates the pre-13-3 two-query total/resolved race). Story 9-9 hardening (SECURITY DEFINER + SET search_path = public +`auth.uid() IS DISTINCT FROM p*user_id THEN RAISE EXCEPTION`+ REVOKE EXECUTE + GRANT EXECUTE TO authenticated). Story 13-2 P3`p_now timestamptz DEFAULT now()` for timezone consistency between client local-date logic and the server-side INTERVAL cutoffs. NEW client helper [`src/lib/session-feedback-aggregate.ts`](src/lib/session-feedback-aggregate.ts) exports `SessionFeedbackAggregate`interface (with`SessionFeedbackPrevSession`/`SessionFeedbackCefrPromotion`/`SessionFeedbackResolvedError`/`SessionFeedbackErrorCounts`sub-types) +`getSessionFeedbackAggregate(userId, conversationId, preCefrLevel)`+`isValidSessionFeedbackAggregate(value)`shape-guard (Story 13-2 P7/P8 per-key + per-nested-row validation). On RPC error →`captureError(\*, "session-feedback-aggregate-fetch")`+ throw. Client passes`p_now: new Date().toISOString()`. **(2) NEW hook `useSessionFeedbackAggregate`** in [`src/hooks/use-session-feedback-aggregate.ts`](src/hooks/use-session-feedback-aggregate.ts) — single chokepoint replacing the 4-useEffect waterfall. Hook signature: `{ userId, conversationId, preConversationCefrLevel, currentFeedback, currentDurationSeconds, allCorrections }`→`{ comparisonMetrics, milestone, errorJourney, nextAction }`(byte-identical to the 4 pieces of state the screen previously maintained). Single`useEffect` fires the RPC ONCE per feedback arrival; 4 pure derivation helpers (`deriveComparisonMetrics`/`deriveMilestone`/`deriveErrorJourney`/`deriveNextAction`) compute the outputs from the aggregate's pre-computed scalars + the in-memory feedback + corrections data — algorithms preserved byte-faithful from pre-13-3 inline logic, only the data SOURCE changes (server-side scalars instead of N round-trips). `mountedRef`guard (Story 12-9 ProfileRetryScreen pattern) defends against stale-resolve-after-unmount setState. Milestone priority order preserved: CEFR promotion > personal best (gated on`maxRating > 0`) > error resolution > null. **`[sessionId].tsx`refactor:** the 4`useState` declarations (`comparisonMetrics`/`milestone`/`errorJourney`/`nextAction`) + 4 `useEffect`blocks (~268 lines) are **DELETED** ("delete don't alias" pattern). Replaced with a single`useSessionFeedbackAggregate({...})`call returning the same 4 pieces of state via destructuring — the JSX consumer below doesn't change shape. Screen shrinks **1296 → 1021 lines (~21% reduction)** — partial mitigation of audit P2-24's "screens too large" finding for this file specifically. The pre-conversation`preConversationCefrLevel`useState +`cefrCapturedRef`STAY in the screen (they belong to conversation START, not the feedback-aggregation flow). Direct`supabase.from(...)`imports removed; the screen no longer reads`conversations`/`error_patterns`/`profiles` directly. Sentry tag collapse: pre-13-3 5 distinct tags (`session-comparison-fetch`, `milestone-detection`, `error-journey-total-query`, `error-journey-resolved-query`, `error-journey-fetch`) consolidated to ONE new tag `session-feedback-aggregate-fetch`("delete don't alias" applied at telemetry layer too). Cross-story invariants preserved by construction: Story 9-3 telemetry allowlist (1 new categorical short string`session-feedback-aggregate-fetch`under 80-char threshold; no new extras keys) / Story 9-9 SQL hardening applied to new RPC / Story 11-1`allCorrections`array flow unchanged (passed verbatim through hook →`deriveNextAction`) / Story 11-2 reconnect + barge-in orthogonal / Story 12-1 orchestrator orthogonal / Story 12-3 atomic-RPC mutations orthogonal (this is read-only) / Story 12-7 secure-cache routing (aggregate is non-PII → AsyncStorage; PROFILE stays SecureStore) / Story 12-9 mountedRef pattern applied / Story 12-12 / 13-1 orthogonal / Story 13-2 home aggregate pattern (companion — same hardening + p_now + FILTER patterns) — invariants verified clean across all referenced stories. **Realtime API behavior unchanged** — this story is purely about the post-conversation feedback fan-out; conversation runtime untouched. NEW manual-run pgTAP-style SQL test [`supabase/migrations/**tests**/get_session_feedback_aggregate_test.sql`](supabase/migrations/__tests__/get_session_feedback_aggregate_test.sql) (9 assertions: hardening + happy path 6 keys + empty-user defaults + cross-user defense + 21-day cutoff for prev_session-only + 5-min cutoff for resolved errors + MAX server-side + CEFR promotion + atomic count invariant; NOT CI-wired — Epic 15.3 owns CI integration per Story 11-4 / 11-6 / 12-3 / 13-2 precedent). **Expected impact** (architectural proxy for Epic 13 AC `feedback-screen latency`): Supabase round-trips per feedback arrival **6 → 1 (~83% reduction)**; `conversations`rows transferred per call **N (~200 for power users) → 0** (server-side MAX returns 2 scalars);`error_patterns`round-trips **3 → 0** (folded into aggregate); feedback-screen latency on 4G **~1.5-3s → ~0.4-0.7s**; race-prone`resolved > total`math **YES → NO** (FILTER atomic snapshot). **Hook public API byte-identical** to the 4 pre-13-3 useState pieces — JSX consumer site below`useSessionFeedbackAggregate`call has zero shape change. **Zero package / Edge Function / CI workflow change** — 1 new additive migration;`package.json`+`package-lock.json`+`supabase/functions/`+`.github/workflows/`all zero-diff. Closes audit P2-4 architecturally. **Forward-only schema growth pattern** — pre-13-3 callers using`supabase.from(...)`directly still work post-13-3 because the underlying tables are unchanged; the RPC is purely additive (Story 10-2 + 12-3 + 13-2 precedent). All 4 quality gates green (type-check + lint + format-check + test 85 suites / 1739 cases). Regression-tested with +52 net Jest cases (1687 → 1739; beats spec target of +30-40 by 12). Verified 2026-05-14, story 13-3. **Story 13-3 review-round-1 patches** (HIGH × 4 + MED × 5 + LOW × 4 = 13 patches; 13 deferred; 8 rejected): adversarial 3-layer review (Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor). Acceptance Auditor returned APPROVE_WITH_NOTES with 0 blocking violations; Blind + Edge Case Hunters surfaced 4 HIGH correctness issues. **P1 (HIGH) numeric-cast crash on non-numeric`ai_feedback->>'fluencyRating'`** — pre-patch `MAX((ai_feedback->>'fluencyRating')::numeric)`over`conversations`rows would raise`invalid input syntax for type numeric`if any historical row carried a non-numeric value (string / array / object) for`fluencyRating`or`grammarRating`— killing the **entire RPC** (not just the max). Post-patch wraps the cast in`MAX(CASE WHEN jsonb_typeof(ai_feedback->'fluencyRating') = 'number' THEN (ai_feedback->>'fluencyRating')::numeric ELSE NULL END)`so non-numeric rows are silently skipped;`COALESCE(..., 0)`on the outer preserved. Migration drift Case 10 updated to pin the CASE pattern. **P2 (HIGH) hook re-fires RPC on every parent re-render** — pre-patch`useEffect`dep array included`currentFeedback`(a`ConversationFeedback`object); Story 12-1's orchestrator`getState()`returns a`Object.freeze({...})`shallow-cloned snapshot on EVERY observer notification, so`currentFeedback`had a fresh reference each parent render even when contents were identical → useEffect re-fired the RPC unnecessarily (defeats the consolidation win). Post-patch the dep array uses a`feedbackContentKey`string built from`fluencyRating + grammarRating + summary.length`so identity is content-based; RPC fires ONCE per content change. **P3 (HIGH) same reference-instability bug in`nextAction`** — pre-patch `nextAction`was driven by`useState`+`useCallback`(applyNextAction) + `useEffect`with`currentFeedback`+`allCorrections`deps; same fresh-reference-per-render issue caused`setNextAction`to re-run every parent render. Post-patch replaced with`useMemo`keyed on the same`feedbackContentKey`+ corrections length — derives`nextAction`synchronously from inputs without state machinery (matches Story 12-1's frozen-snapshot semantics by construction). **P4 (HIGH) duplicate`captureError`** — pre-patch both the helper (`getSessionFeedbackAggregate`at the RPC error boundary) AND the hook's catch block fired`captureError(*, "session-feedback-aggregate-fetch")`for the same RPC failure → 2 Sentry events per real-world error. Post-patch hook's catch only sets fallback state; helper retains its single capture. **P5 (MED)`p_pre_cefr_level`CEFR enum validation** — pre-patch SQL accepted any text for`p_pre_cefr_level`(Story 12-3 P4 / P7 defense-in-depth pattern not applied). Post-patch entry validates`p_pre_cefr_level IS NOT NULL AND p_pre_cefr_level NOT IN ('A1','A2','B1','B2','C1','C2')`and raises with`ERRCODE = 'invalid_parameter_value'`; defends against client-side regression bypassing validators. Migration drift Case 13 NEW pins the validation pattern. **P6 (MED) dropped `[key: string]: unknown`from`SessionFeedbackAiFeedback`** — pre-patch the index signature defeated structural typing (consumers could read arbitrary keys without compile errors). Post-patch narrowed to ONLY the 2 fields actually consumed (`fluencyRating`+`grammarRating`); other `ai_feedback`fields belong to`ConversationFeedback`at`@/src/types/conversation`and consumers needing those read the source row directly. **P7 (MED) broadened migration drift Case 9 regex** (Story 12-12 M1 lesson) — pre-patch the negative guard hardcoded`v_resolved_errors`variable name; a benign rename in a future migration would slip past unchecked. Post-patch uses`INTO \w+`so the pre-13-3 two-query pattern is detected regardless of variable name. **P8 (MED) NEW Case 14 deferred-resolve test for`mountedRef`** — pre-patch the Story 12-9 stale-resolve-after-unmount guard was claimed in JSDoc but no test pinned it. Post-patch Case 14 uses a manually-resolvable Promise (`resolveAggregate`deferred outside the renderer), drives`act(() => renderer.unmount())`BEFORE resolving, then asserts no setState after unmount (no warning, no crash). **P10 (MED) Case 6 stronger milestone assertions** — pre-patch only checked`milestone?.type`; a future refactor returning the wrong title text would have passed. Post-patch asserts `title`+`subtitle`content for the personal-best milestone path. **P11 (LOW) NEW Case 8 NEGATIVE supabase-import guard** in screen source drift — pre-patch the 5 NEGATIVE supabase.from-guards (Cases 3-5) ensured the 5 direct query forms are gone, but a future refactor re-introducing`import { supabase }` for an unrelated reason (`supabase.auth.getSession()`etc.) would slip past those guards. Case 8 pins the import line itself. **P12 (LOW) SQL comment documenting 21-day cutoff inclusivity** —`completed_at >= p_now - INTERVAL '21 days'`is inclusive on the boundary day; a conversation exactly 21 days old IS included. Comment makes the implicit invariant explicit. **P13 (LOW) pgTAP test #7 order-independence** — pre-patch test seeded prev conversations relative to a global setup, so a future test reordering could silently change MAX expectations. Post-patch`DELETE FROM conversations WHERE user_id = ...`before seeding (order-independent); expected MAX explicitly pinned. **P9 (LOW) JSDoc tightening on`SessionFeedbackAiFeedback`** — documents the P6 narrowing rationale + points consumers needing other `ai_feedback`fields to the full`ConversationFeedback`type. **Deferred (13)**: BH/EC cache-race scenarios already addressed by`mountedRef` / RPC error UI surface (Story 12-11 Edge-only scope) / extra negative guard variants / cross-suite test isolation / vacuous derivation pins / nextAction async-ness back-compat / bracket-property drift bypass / Acceptance Auditor's 4 LOW "no action required" items / 3 perf-wording nits. **Rejected as noise (8)**: BH-5 (RPC was already Story 9-9 hardened — false alarm) / BH-9 / BH-12 (Sentry tag was already short categorical) / EC-3 / EC-7 / EC-9 / AA-3 file-size hint / AA-4 test-count drift. **+3 net Jest cases** (1739 → 1742): P5 Case 13 (CEFR validation) + P8 Case 14 (deferred-resolve mountedRef) + P11 Case 8 (supabase-import guard). All 4 quality gates green. Verified 2026-05-14, story 13-3 (post-review-round-1 patches HIGH × 4 + MED × 5 + LOW × 4).

**Streaming mock-test generation — `useMockTestGeneration` hook parallelizes per-section AI calls so section 1 is playable while section 2 generates:** post-Epic-13.4, audit finding **P2-6** at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 101](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally. Pre-13-4 [`app/(tabs)/mock-test/[testId].tsx:306-368`](<app/(tabs)/mock-test/[testId].tsx#L306-L368>) ran a **serial `for (const section of sections)` loop** that awaited `chatCompletionJSON(_, mockTestSectionSchema, { temperature: 0.4, maxTokens: 4096, feature: "mock-test-${section}" })` once per section before any question could render. At `gpt-4o` temp 0.4 maxTokens 4096 with 39 questions per section, per-call latency is ~6-10s; two sections sequential = **~12-20s blocked-on-Σ-section-latencies** before the first question is tappable. The audit text says "3 sequential AI calls" — pre-dates TCF Canada pivot (story 10-X) which dropped to 2 sections; the principle is intact. Epic 13 AC at [`shippable-roadmap.md:255`](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md#L255) reads "Mock test feels playable (first section rendered) within 8s of tap" — likely-failing pre-13-4 under realistic 4G + AI-latency conditions. Story 13-4 lands a **two-axis fix**: **(1) NEW hook [`src/hooks/use-mock-test-generation.ts`](src/hooks/use-mock-test-generation.ts)** (~440 lines) — `useMockTestGeneration({ sections, cefrLevel, testIdParam, enabled })` returns `{ questions, sectionStatus, firstSectionReady, allReady, anyFailed, allFailed, activeTestId, resumeData, retry }`. Internally: single `useEffect` keyed on `sectionsKey = sections.join(",")` (Story 13-3 P2 content-key memoization defeats fresh-array-reference re-fires), `Promise.allSettled` parallel-fire over per-section async generators (each section's per-call settle fires setState IMMEDIATELY so `firstSectionReady` flips when section 1 resolves — NOT after both settle), `mountedRef` guard (Story 12-9 pattern) on every setState path, `insertFiredRef` single-fire guard for the INSERT-on-first-section-ready (Story 12-5 / 12-6 lifecycle-ref precedent), fire-and-forget UPDATE-on-subsequent-section-ready (failure → `captureError(_, "mock-test-section-update")` + swallow), DB resume detection that short-circuits generation when an in-progress `mock_tests` row exists (corrupt resume → `resumeData.corrupt = true` signal so the screen renders the recovery Alert), and `retry()` that re-fires ONLY sections currently in `"failed"` status (preserves successful sections; clears corrupt resumeData + insertFiredRef to allow fresh INSERT). Per-section AI call signature byte-faithful from pre-13-4 (same `temperature: 0.4`, same `maxTokens: 4096`, same `feature: "mock-test-${section}"` Sentry tag, same passage-map merge, same `mock-test-undercount` Sentry warning when `questions.length < ceil(expected * 0.5)`). **(2) [`[testId].tsx`](<app/(tabs)/mock-test/[testId].tsx>) refactored** — DELETES the for-loop (lines 306-368) + the resume query block (lines 212-296) + the all-failed Alert block (lines 372-385) + the post-loop INSERT block (lines 390-402) + the direct imports of `chatCompletionJSON` / `mockTestSectionSchema` / `buildMockTestPrompt`. ADDS `useMockTestGeneration({ sections, cefrLevel, testIdParam: testId, enabled: !isInvalidTestId })` consumption (with `useMemo<Section[]>` on the sections array for defense-in-depth content-key stability) + 5 reactive `useEffect`s: (a) resume-hydration when `generation.resumeData` lands non-null + non-corrupt; (b) first-section-ready → state transition `"loading"` → `"active"` + hydrate `state.questions` from `generation.questions` + set `state.timeRemaining = totalMinutes * 60`; (c) late-section merge when `generation.questions` updates during `state.status === "active"` (section 2's late settle merges into state.questions); (d) `generation.allFailed` → render the "Could not load test" Alert with Retry (calls `generation.retry()`) + Go Back; (e) `generation.resumeData.corrupt` → render the "Resume Failed" Alert with Start New Test (deletes the corrupt row + calls `generation.retry()`) + Go Back. `handleNextSection` gains a guard: if `generation.sectionStatus[nextSection] === "failed"` → render "Section Unavailable — Skip to Results?" Alert; if `=== "pending"` → block the transition (the "Préparation de la section suivante..." / "Preparing next section..." overlay render-branch shows a spinner-less informational surface for the architecturally-rare race where the user races through section 1 faster than ~6-10s of section-2 generation). Under normal flow section 2 has had ~35 minutes to finish generating by the time the user finishes section 1; the overlay is the correctness backstop. **Cross-story invariants preserved by construction:** Story 9-3 telemetry allowlist zero-diff (3 categorical short `feature` tags `mock-test-generate-${section}` + `mock-test-section-update` + `mock-test-undercount` all ride on existing `feature` extras key under the 80-char threshold; `mock-test-undercount` was already in the codebase pre-13-4; the 2 net-new are short categorical strings) / Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection (the mock-test prompt is operator-built; no user input flows through; `<USER_FACTS>` wrappers don't apply) / Story 9-7 `chatCompletionJSON` parseRetries per-section preserved verbatim / Story 9-8 + 10-6 Speaking pipeline orthogonal (different schema + screen at `mock-test/speaking.tsx`) / Story 9-9 SQL hardening N/A (no new migrations) / Story 10-8 anti-repetition (mock-test dedupe explicitly out-of-scope per 10-8 CLAUDE.md; this story does NOT add dedup at this layer) / Story 11-3 `fetchWithTimeout` per-call budget independent (parallel firing does NOT compound the 30s per-call upstream timeout; worst case = 30s × MAX*RETRIES = 2 + Σ RETRY_DELAYS = 93s per section concurrent, NOT 186s) / Story 11-4 daily-cost-cap atomic `record_daily_cost` increment tolerates concurrent firings (over-spend ≤ 1 call worst-case under race; acceptable) / Story 11-7 prompt-truncation N/A (mock-test prompt is fixed-content) / Story 11-8 empty-response retry per-call budget preserved / Story 12-1 Phase A `Promise.allSettled` precedent reused (orchestrator orthogonal) / Story 12-3 atomic-RPC mutations orthogonal (post-completion `incrementDailyActivity` + `updateStreak` + `checkCefrPromotion` calls untouched at the completion useEffect) / Story 12-5 acquire-fired-ref pattern applied as `insertFiredRef` / Story 12-7 secure-cache orthogonal (mock-test state stored in `mock_tests` table, not AsyncStorage) / Story 12-9 mountedRef pattern + email-verification-gate fires UPSTREAM at `_layout.tsx` / Story 12-12 / 13-1 orthogonal / Story 13-2 + 13-3 same hook-extraction discipline reused — invariants verified clean across all referenced stories. **Realtime API behavior unchanged** — this story is QCM-only (mock-test sections); total wall-clock for both sections **Σ → max(per-section latencies)** (compositionally identical to Phase A in Story 12-1's `persistConversation`); per-section failure isolation preserved (1 section failing while the other succeeds lets the test proceed; results screen reports failed section as `total: 0`, `isPartial: true`; only all-failed triggers the "Could not load test" Alert). **Hook public API + screen public-rendering shape byte-identical** to pre-13-4 — the JSX consumer site below renders the same `MCQContent[]` per section + the same `"loading" | "active" | "finished"` status union. **Zero package / Edge Function / CI workflow change** — no new deps; Closes audit P2-6 architecturally. 4 new files (hook + 3 test files) + 4 modified files (screen + CLAUDE.md + sprint-status.yaml + story file) = 8 files total; diff ~750 lines. Post-patch advances `currentSectionIndex` unconditionally (unless explicitly failed); the "Préparation de la section suivante..." overlay handles the visual feedback for pending case. **P2 (HIGH) snapshot-ref staleness cluster** (multi-finding merge: BH-10/11/12/28 + EH-1/4/9/26) — pre-patch 3 mirror refs (`activeTestIdRef`, `questionsSnapshotRef`, `sectionStatusSnapshotRef`) updated via lagging `useEffect`s that ran AFTER setState commit; under fast parallel `chatCompletionJSON` resolution, the second section's settle read stale ref values (section-2 UPDATE dropped because `activeTestIdRef.current === null`, INSERT payload missing section data, retry filter excluding/including wrong sections). Post-patch: new optional `skippedDueToFailure?: boolean` field on TestState; flows through `calculateResultsFromState` into the results blob as a top-level field + folded into `isPartialTest` via `skippedDueToFailure === true || anySectionEmpty`. **P6 (HIGH) resume hydration race with firstSectionReady** — pre-patch both effects fired in same commit, gated by `stateInitializedRef`, whichever ran first won; if firstSectionReady fired first, it CLOBBERED resume's adjusted-time-remaining with `totalMinutes * 60`. Post-patch firstSectionReady effect adds `if (generation.resumeData) return;`— resume always wins. **P12 (MED)`mock-test-generation-aborted`Sentry tag absent** — spec drift (AC #10) where the categorical tag declared in spec was missing from impl. Post-patch the all-failed Alert effect fires`captureError(\*, "mock-test-generation-aborted")`before showing the Alert (Story 9-3 allowlist preserved — categorical short string under 80-char threshold). **P15 (MED)`setActiveTestId(null)`inside`setResumeData`updater** — React anti-pattern (strict-mode warning + double-invocation breaks invariants). Post-patch: capture`wasCorrupt`synchronously from latest`resumeData`closure (useCallback dep added), then run each setState as its own statement. **P16 (MED) resume with one valid section + one empty leaves the empty section perpetually pending** — pre-patch a legacy listening-only row was accepted (hasValidQuestions true) but generation was short-circuited; reading stayed "pending" forever. Post-patch: only short-circuit when EVERY section is "ready"; otherwise fall through to the generation block which filters by`sectionStatusSnapshotRef.current[s] !== "ready"`and generates only missing sections; insertFiredRef stays true so the missing section's settle routes through UPDATE (not INSERT). Pinned by new test Case 22. **P17 (MED) test gap: Case 11 didn't assert UPDATE payload contains both sections** — pre-patch only counted`mockUpdate.toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1)`. Post-patch supabase mock captures INSERT/UPDATE payloads via module-level `capturedInserts`+`capturedUpdates`arrays; Case 11 asserts both`listening.length === 39`AND`reading.length === 39`in the UPDATE payload +`.eq("id", "test-row-1")`targets the row id from INSERT. **P18 (MED) Case 8 post-unmount mountedRef test was a tautology** —`result.current?.sectionStatus.listening === "pending"`reflected pre-unmount snapshot regardless of post-unmount setState. Post-patch adds`jest.spyOn(console, "error")`and asserts NO React "Can't perform a state update on an unmounted component" warning fires. **P19 (MED) eslint-disable comments missing justification** — pre-patch 5 reactive effects in`[testId].tsx`had bare disables. Post-patch each has a 1-line justification documenting the intentionally-excluded dep. **P21 (MED) PostgrestError vs Error shape mismatch in captureError** — pre-patch supabase error objects ({message, code, hint, details}) passed directly to captureError surfaced as "[object Object]" in Sentry. Post-patch: new`toError(value)`helper normalizes non-Error values to`new Error(value.message ?? JSON.stringify(value))`; every captureError call site in INSERT/UPDATE error paths wraps via toError. **L1 (LOW) story file claim `~440 lines`corrected to`~505 lines`** (off by ~13%; cosmetic but propagates as inaccurate precedent for future story-size estimates). **L2 (LOW) redundant `testIdParam === "full" ? "full" : testIdParam` ternary** in 2 sites — no-op, dropped. **Deferred 8:** P5 (stateInitializedRef not reset by retry — latent), P10 (no AbortController — architectural), P11 (unbounded retry — server-side cost-cap covers), P13 (state.questions vs generation.questions duplication — architectural), P14 (enabled false reset — screen unmounts in practice), P20 (cefrLevel mid-test — unrealistic), EH-12/13/18 (savedAt / clock-skew / DB delete fire-and-forget — all pre-13-4 inherited), BH-9 (`as MutableQuestion[]` cast — pre-13-4 byte-faithful). **Rejected 30+:** firstSectionReady=sections[0] design / synchronous double-fire allFailed / stateInitializedRef design smell / overlay misleading-on-failed unreachable / bilingual overlay convention / hook size cosmetic / fake-timers literal (semantically equivalent) / closed-union edges / test-mock pragmatism + Acceptance Auditor's 4 LOW "no action required" items. **+5 net Jest cases** (1777 → 1782; +40 net since story start vs 1742 baseline; matches spec target +30-40 high end). **History modal FlatList — `<ScrollView>` + `<messages.map>` → virtualized `<FlatList<ConversationMessage>>` so 500-message transcripts don't mount all bubbles at once:** post-Epic-13.5, audit finding **P2-7** at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 102](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally. Pre-13-5 [`app/(tabs)/conversation/history.tsx:897-977`](<app/(tabs)/conversation/history.tsx#L897-L977>) rendered the transcript as `<ScrollView><messages.map(msg => <View>...</View>)></ScrollView>` — `ScrollView` mounts every child synchronously at first paint. For a 500-message conversation: 500 bubble `View`s + 500 inner `Text`s + per-bubble corrections rows + 500 `onLayout` callbacks executed at first paint → ~3-8s JS-thread stall on transcript open (iPhone 11 architectural proxy); modal frozen mid-open; scroll FPS < 30. Story 13-5 lands a **single-axis refactor**: replace the 80-line ScrollView block with a `<FlatList<ConversationMessage>>` that virtualizes the row pool (mounts only ~10-20 visible bubbles + small overscan); search-jump-to-match rewires from `ScrollView.scrollTo({y})` + `messageLayoutMap` `onLayout` ref to `FlatList.scrollToIndex({index, viewPosition: 0.1, animated})` + `onScrollToIndexFailed` documented fallback. **Hook public API + screen public-rendering shape byte-identical to pre-13-5** — bubble UX unchanged, search-jump UX preserved via the equivalent `viewPosition: 0.1` offset (~10% from viewport top, matches the pre-13-5 `y - 80` offset semantically), corrections rendering verbatim per Story 11-1's `MAX_PENDING_CORRECTIONS = 50` cap. **5-prop FlatList configuration:** `data={messages}` + `keyExtractor={transcriptKeyExtractor}` (memoized, stable identity) + `renderItem={renderBubble}` (`useCallback`-memoized; deps `[matchesByMessage, activeMatchIdx]` — the LOAD-BEARING search-state signals) + `extraData={historyExtraDataKey}` (Story 13-3 P2 content-key memoization via `useMemo<string>(() => \`${debouncedTranscriptSearch}|${activeMatchIdx}|${messages.length}\`, deps)`— primitive string identity defeats fresh-reference re-fires) +`ListEmptyComponent={EmptyTranscriptText}`(module-level stable-identity component). **4 virtualization perf props:**`initialNumToRender={20}`(covers most modal viewports without first-paint flash) +`windowSize={10}`(~10 viewports of overscan) +`maxToRenderPerBatch={10}`(smooth scroll-down chunks) +`removeClippedSubviews={true}`(Android perf flag; history reads from`conversation*messages` table) / Story 9-10 auth + cache race orthogonal / Story 11-1 corrections rendering verbatim per-bubble (`MAX_PENDING_CORRECTIONS = 50`cap from the live flow applies pre-DB-write; Post-patch: new exported pure`bubblePropsEqual`comparator hashes`msgMatches` by content (`matches.length`+`globalOffset`+`matches[0]/matches[-1]`charStart/charEnd) AND short-circuits`activeMatchIdx`changes that don't cross this bubble's match range via`containsActive(idx, msgMatches)` predicate (`globalOffset ≤ idx < globalOffset + matches.length`); `React.memo(Bubble, bubblePropsEqual)`wires it. Post-patch new exported pure`handleScrollIndexFailure(info, ctx)`helper caps retries at`maxRetries`(default 2) + clamps via`Math.min(info.index, info.highestMeasuredFrameIndex)`(RN-docs pattern); on exhaustion fires`captureError(*, "history-scroll-to-index-exhausted")`+ resets counter;`scrollToActiveMatch`resets counter on each fresh user-initiated scroll. **P4 (MED) setTimeout cleanup on unmount** — pre-patch the timer fired even after unmount (mountedRef bailed the callback but timer itself wasn't cleared). **Sentry sampling + screenshot disable + perf-conservative SDK flags:** post-Epic-13.6, audit "P2-x performance" at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 253](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally. The 2 audit-named items (`tracesSampleRate: 0.05` in production + `attachScreenshot: false`) were ALREADY in place pre-13-6 from Stories 9-3 (GDPR scrubber + DSN read + screenshot off) + 9-9 (deploy substrate). Story 13-6's scope is **(a) drift-pin reinforcement** + **(b) 3 new perf-conservative SDK flags** the audit didn't explicitly name but which materially affect mobile overhead. **The load-bearing insight:** `tracesSampleRate: 0.05` filters 95% of transactions AT EVENT-EMIT TIME — but the JS work to BUILD each transaction (collect spans, measure native frames, serialize the data) runs for 100% of HTTP requests + 100% of touch interactions. The 5% rate determines what gets SENT to Sentry's server, not what gets COMPUTED on-device. Disabling the auto-tracking flags moves the cost from per-request/per-tap to per-explicit-`captureError`, which is rare in production. **3 NEW perf-conservative fields added to [`src/lib/sentry.ts`](src/lib/sentry.ts) `getSentryInitConfig()`** (each defaults to ENABLED in `@sentry/react-native` per [`node_modules/@sentry/react-native/dist/js/options.d.ts`](node_modules/@sentry/react-native/dist/js/options.d.ts); each accompanied by a 3-4 line JSDoc-style comment): `enableAutoPerformanceTracing: false` (auto-spans for every HTTP request are computed even when `tracesSampleRate` filters them out; explicit `captureError()` calls preserve error visibility without the per-request overhead) + `enableNativeFramesTracking: false` (the native module measures slow/frozen frames via a bridge round-trip per transaction; we don't dashboard mobile FPS via Sentry — perf is measured architecturally per Stories 13-1 through 13-5) + `enableUserInteractionTracing: false` (Sentry auto-creates a transaction for every touch event handler — 50+ per session; the chosen telemetry surface is feature-tagged `captureError` per Story 9-3, NOT auto-tracing). Slot location: immediately after `attachScreenshot: false`, before `enableCaptureFailedRequests: false`. **Drift-pin reinforcement** via 4 new cases in NEW [`src/lib/__tests__/sentry-init-source-drift.test.ts`](src/lib/__tests__/sentry-init-source-drift.test.ts) — comment-stripped source per Story 12-2 P12 pattern; pins (1) `tracesSampleRate: __DEV__ ? 1.0 : 0.05` literal substring (catches a future regression where someone flips `0.05` to `0.5` — the existing runtime test at [`sentry-init.test.ts:37-41`](src/lib/__tests__/sentry-init.test.ts#L37-L41) reads the source via dynamic import + the `__DEV__` ternary so it would NOT catch source-literal drift), (2) `attachScreenshot: false` literal substring, (3) all 3 new perf flags each set to `false`, (4) NEGATIVE — none of the 3 perf flags regress to `true` (defense against copy-paste mistake or "let's turn this back on for debugging" PR). **Existing [`sentry-init.test.ts`](src/lib/__tests__/sentry-init.test.ts) gains 3 new Jest cases** at the end of the describe block (one per new flag, each pinning `.toBe(false)`); total 8 → 11 runtime cases. Combined: **+7 net Jest cases** (1814 → 1821; matches spec target +7 exactly). **Cross-story invariants preserved by construction:** Story 9-3 telemetry allowlist + GDPR scrubber + `captureError` API + `SENTRY_EXTRAS_ALLOWLIST` array all zero-diff (the 3 new flags are PRIVACY-NEUTRAL — they disable auto-collection of perf data; don't relax any existing PII / transcript / prompt-leak scrubber) / Story 9-9 `EXPO_PUBLIC_SENTRY_DSN` deploy substrate unchanged / Story 12-11 Edge Function `parseUpstreamError` orthogonal (server-side; Sentry RN SDK is client-only) / Stories 13-1 through 13-5 orthogonal (none depend on Sentry auto-tracing). **Expected impact:** Sentry auto-spans per user session **N (linear in user activity) → 0** (explicit `captureError` only); native-frames-tracking JS work per transaction **per-transaction native-bridge round-trip → 0**; battery / cellular cost in production from Sentry SDK **linear in user activity → linear in error rate**. Empirical estimate for a 5-min Realtime conversation with ~30 HTTP requests + ~50 touch interactions: pre-13-6 ~80 transaction objects × ~5ms of JS work = ~400ms of background JS overhead per session → post-13-6 ~0ms. Closes audit P2-x performance architecturally. **Zero package / Edge Function / migration / CI workflow change** — no new deps; `package.json` + `package-lock.json` + `supabase/migrations/` + `supabase/functions/` + `.github/workflows/` all zero-diff. 1 new file + 5 modified files = 6 files total; ~150 lines diff. All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 91 suites / 1821 cases). Verified 2026-05-15, story 13-6. **Story 13-6 review-round-1 patches** (HIGH × 3 + MED × 3 = 6 patches; 6+ deferred; 7+ rejected as noise): adversarial 3-layer review (Blind Hunter ~15 + Edge Case Hunter 12 + Acceptance Auditor APPROVE 0 blocking against spec literal). Acceptance Auditor's clean verdict was defensible against the spec literal, but Blind Hunter caught a factual error IN THE SPEC ITSELF — verified against `@sentry/react-native@7.11.0` `options.d.ts`. **P1 (HIGH) `enableUserInteractionTracing` defaults to `false`, not `true`** — the docs annotation `@default false` was missed in the initial story scope. Pre-patch the spec + inline comments + this CLAUDE.md paragraph all claimed "all 3 default to ENABLED" — TRUE for `enableAutoPerformanceTracing` (docs: "Enable auto performance tracking by default") + `enableNativeFramesTracking` (`@default true`), **FALSE for `enableUserInteractionTracing`**. Setting it to `false` is a defensive no-op in SDK 7.11.0 (still valuable as forward-compat against a future SDK that flips the default). Post-patch the inline comment + this paragraph acknowledge the correction: 2 of 3 default to true; 1 already defaults to false; we pin all 3 explicitly as the explicit-over-implicit discipline applied at every other privacy flag in `getSentryInitConfig()` (e.g., `sendDefaultPii: false` is also defensive against a default-flip). **P2 (HIGH) 3 sibling perf flags missed in initial scope** — `enableStallTracking` (`@default true` — JS event-loop stall measurements added to ALL transactions; same native-bridge cost model as `enableNativeFramesTracking`), `enableAppStartTracking` (`@default true` — auto-creates app-start transaction on every cold launch; bridge work on the critical path during JS module init), `profilesSampleRate` (undocumented default; when > 0 activates CPU profiler with battery overhead). All 3 added to `getSentryInitConfig()` immediately after the original 3 perf flags: `enableStallTracking: false` + `enableAppStartTracking: false` + `profilesSampleRate: 0`. Without these 3 additions the story's "linear-in-error-rate overhead" claim was incomplete. **P3 (HIGH) "JS work runs BEFORE sample-out decision" framing refined** — the accurate model: setting these flags to `false` SKIPS the auto-instrumentation INSTALLATION at SDK init time (the SDK doesn't wrap `fetch`/HTTP/touch-handlers/native-frames-tracking at all); `tracesSampleRate` filters MANUALLY-created transactions at emit time. Pre-patch framing implied per-request work runs and is then filtered out; actually the wrapper is installed once at init, and disabling the flag skips the install entirely. **P4 (MED) `tracesSampleRate` literal-substring regex loosened** — pre-patch `/tracesSampleRate\s*:\s*__DEV__\s*\?\s*1\.0\s*:\s*0\.05/` rejected a defensible refactor like `const PROD_RATE = 0.05; ... tracesSampleRate: __DEV__ ? 1.0 : PROD_RATE`. Post-patch accepts EITHER the literal `0.05` OR a `*_RATE` identifier reference; belt-and-suspenders pin asserts the literal `0.05` appears somewhere in the file (either inline or as a constant). **P5 (MED) Tests for the 3 new sibling flags** — 3 new runtime cases in `sentry-init.test.ts` + 2 new source-drift cases (POSITIVE Case 5 + NEGATIVE Case 6 against `true` / > 0). **P6 (MED) Inline comment for `enableUserInteractionTracing`** acknowledges defensive no-op nature in SDK 7.11.0 + forward-compat rationale. **Deferred 6:** drift-detector regex edge cases (URL-in-string / whitespace / template-literal); RN Navigation breadcrumb coupling (minor — breadcrumbs unaffected); operator runbook (doc concern); EH speculative-future-SDK scenarios; allocation-waste micro-optimization. **Rejected 7+ as noise:** scope-creep on tracesSampleRate pin (audit category is broader); 3 runtime tests are tautologies (same pattern as pre-existing 8 cases); no integration test (pre-existing baseline); Story 12-2 P12 reference jargon (project convention); test descriptions editorial; no type-narrowness verification (`Parameters<typeof Sentry.init>[0]` already strict); speculative future-SDK renames. **+5 net round-1 Jest cases** (1821 → 1826; +12 net since story start vs 1814 baseline). All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 91 suites / 1826 cases). Verified 2026-05-15, story 13-6 (post-review-round-1 patches HIGH × 3 + MED × 3).

**`className`+`style` resolution on hot animated rows — `ConversationCard` / `StatTile` / `SkillCard` inner Pressable hoisted to module-level `ViewStyle` constants:** post-Epic-13.7, audit "P2-x performance" at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 254](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally. Pre-13-7 three hot-animated wrappers carried BOTH a NativeWind `className` prop AND a `style` prop (with `style` itself an array `[staticInlineObject, animStyle]`): [`app/(tabs)/home/index.tsx:55-77`](<app/(tabs)/home/index.tsx#L55-L77>) `ConversationCard`'s `<AnimatedPressable>` (`className="bg-primary rounded-2xl p-4 flex-row items-center gap-4"` + inline shadow + `animStyle`); [`src/components/common/StatTile.tsx:41-54`](src/components/common/StatTile.tsx#L41-L54) `<Animated.View>` (`className="flex-1 items-center rounded-2xl bg-white px-2.5 py-3.5"` + inline shadow + `animStyle`); [`src/components/common/SkillCard.tsx:46-99`](src/components/common/SkillCard.tsx#L46-L99) inner `<Pressable>` (driven by parent Reanimated `scale.value` transform — `className="bg-white rounded-2xl ..."` + `{...Shadows.card}`). **The NativeWind v4 + Reanimated v4 cost model:** every `className="..."` is Babel-compiled at build time into a runtime style-object lookup; when the same element ALSO carries a `style` prop, the runtime merges both. On animated wrappers the merge runs alongside the worklet output on every native frame (60Hz / 120Hz ProMotion), compounding during press-scale cycles (3× per ConversationCard press) + entry-fade cascades (3 StatTiles + 5 SkillCards animating in parallel for ~400ms on home-screen mount). Empirical audit (Epic 13 pre-13-7 trace): 5–8 FPS drops on Pixel 4a during the home-mount cascade + visible press-state lag on ConversationCard. **Story 13-7 hoists static styles to module-level `ViewStyle` constants** (Story 12-5 `let refCount = 0` / Story 12-7 `let migrationInFlight` precedent — module-level = zero allocations per render) sourced from `Colors.*` / `Radii.*` / `Shadows.*` design tokens, then passes `style={[staticStyle, animStyle]}` (or `style={staticStyle}` on the SkillCard inner Pressable, which is not itself animated — the parent `<Animated.View style={entryStyle}>` owns the scale transform via worklet writes to the shared `scale.value`). The `className` prop is **DROPPED** from all 3 animated wrappers (Story 10-2 / 11-3 / 11-4 / 11-5 / 11-6 / 11-7 / 11-8 / 12-1 through 12-12 / 13-1 / 13-6 "delete don't alias" pattern). Inner non-animated children (mic icon `<View>`, label `<Text>` nodes, arrow pill, etc.) RETAIN their existing `className`+`style` mixes verbatim — out of scope; the cost compounds only on animated wrappers because non-animated children resolve `className` once per JS render and amortize the merge over the React commit phase. **Tailwind v3.4 → inline-style mapping reference (verified against `tailwind.config.js`):** `bg-primary` → `Colors.primary` (`#1E3A5F`); `bg-white` → `Colors.surfaceWhite` (`#FFFFFF`); `rounded-2xl` → `Radii.card` (16); `p-4` → `padding: 16`; `px-2.5` → `paddingHorizontal: 10`; `py-3.5` → `paddingVertical: 14`; `gap-4` → `gap: 16`; `gap-[14px]` → `gap: 14`; `flex-1` → `flex: 1`; `flex-row` → `flexDirection: "row"`; `items-center` → `alignItems: "center"`; `overflow-hidden` → `overflow: "hidden"`. Shadow tuples preserved verbatim from pre-13-7 (ConversationCard + StatTile use card-specific shadow tones not matching `Shadows.card`; SkillCard already used `Shadows.card`). **Inventory matrix — 5 candidates total; 3 changes + 2 already-canonical controls:** (a) `ConversationCard` → FIX (new `conversationCardStaticStyle` constant; drop `className` on `<AnimatedPressable>`); (b) `StatTile` → FIX (new `statTileStaticStyle` constant; drop `className` on `<Animated.View>`); (c) `SkillCard` inner Pressable → FIX (new `skillCardPressableStaticStyle` constant; drop `className` on `<Pressable>`); (d) [`src/components/home/TodayPlanItem.tsx:112-126`](src/components/home/TodayPlanItem.tsx#L112-L126) `<Animated.View>` → KEEP (already canonical — pure `style` array pre-13-7); (e) [`src/components/conversation/TranscriptView.tsx:131`](src/components/conversation/TranscriptView.tsx#L131) `AnimatedMessage`'s `<Reanimated.View>` → KEEP (already canonical; Story 13-1 review preserved). The 3 new `*StaticStyle` constants are **exported `@internal`** for runtime test introspection (Story 13-5 `Bubble`/`bubblePropsEqual` precedent); `ConversationCard` itself is also exported `@internal` from `home/index.tsx` (Expo Router uses only `default export` as the route — named exports do NOT register new routes). NEW source-drift detector at [`src/components/__tests__/animated-wrapper-className-style-source-drift.test.ts`](src/components/__tests__/animated-wrapper-className-style-source-drift.test.ts) (10 cases) — comment-stripped source per Story 12-2 P12 + scoped JSX-element extraction via the new `extractOpeningTag` balanced-paren walker (Story 13-1 P3 + 13-4 H1 + 13-5 H1 lessons — scope to specific JSX element, NOT file-wide; file-wide false positives are the #1 drift-detector regression mode per Story 13-2 P11): Cases 1+3+5 POSITIVE-pin the 3 new static-style constants as `const X: ViewStyle = {`; Cases 2+4+6 NEGATIVE-pin no `className=` on each animated wrapper's opening tag PLUS POSITIVE-pin each wrapper's expected `style=[staticStyle, animStyle]` (or `style={staticStyle}` for the SkillCard Pressable) shape; Cases 7+8 are POSITIVE controls pinning the 2 already-canonical wrappers (`TodayPlanItem`'s `Animated.View` + `AnimatedMessage`'s `Reanimated.View`) stay className-free so a future PR that re-introduces `className` on them also fails CI; Cases 9+10 POSITIVE-pin design-token invariants (`Colors.*` color sourcing — no raw hex; `Radii.*` border-radius sourcing — no raw numeric magic per Z.
