per-frame work during press-scale animations on `ConversationCard` **~0.10ms × 60 frames/press × N presses → ~0.02ms × N** (residual cost is just the array-merge of `[staticStyle, animStyle]` which Reanimated optimizes via worklet hoisting); home-screen mount FPS on Pixel 4a (architectural proxy) **~50 FPS → ≥ 55 FPS** during the StatTile + SkillCard `withDelay` entry cascade (3 StatTiles + 5 SkillCards = 8 animated wrappers in parallel for ~400ms); visual output **byte-identical pixels** (pure style-resolution refactor — the merged final style is identical between pre-13-7 and post-13-7); bundle size **−0 bytes** (NativeWind className compiles to a runtime lookup; removing it shifts work, not bytes). **0 new packages, 0 migrations, 0 Edge Function changes, 0 CI workflow changes** — load-bearing scope discipline (3 source files modified + 2 new test files + CLAUDE.md + sprint-status + story file = 8 files total; ~400 lines diff). Closes audit P2-x performance architecturally. Regression-tested with **+14 net Jest cases** (1826 → 1840; exceeds spec target +10–14 at the high end): 10 source-drift + 4 runtime smoke. All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 93 suites / 1840 cases). Verified 2026-05-15, story 13-7. **Story 13-7 review-round-1 patches** (HIGH × 3 + MED × 3 = 6 patches; 15 deferred; ~20 rejected as noise): adversarial 3-layer review (Blind Hunter ~30 + Edge Case Hunter 27 + Acceptance Auditor APPROVE 0 blocking). Acceptance Auditor's clean verdict was defensible against the spec literal AND held up under Blind + Edge Case scrutiny — the 6 patches are reinforcement, NOT spec violations. **P1 (HIGH) `Shadows.card` spread moved to TOP of `skillCardPressableStaticStyle`** — pre-patch the spread was LAST and a future `Shadows.card` token-addition (e.g., adding `padding`) would have silently clobbered the explicit `padding: 16` / `gap: 14` settings; post-patch spread-first so explicit settings always win. **P2 (HIGH) all 3 `*StaticStyle` constants wrapped in `Object.freeze(...) as ViewStyle`** — pre-patch mutable module-level objects could be mutated by a debug session / runtime A/B test / future theming code path and silently change EVERY instance globally for the rest of the JS session (Story 12-1 `getState() = Object.freeze({...})` precedent applied). NEW Case 5 pins `Object.isFrozen(constant) === true` + verifies runtime-mutation-attempt is a no-op. **P3 (HIGH) runtime test predicates strengthened** — Case 1 anchors on (Colors.primary background) AND (accessibilityRole === "button"); all 3 cases verify all matching candidates describe ONE logical element by checking the `accessibilityLabel` set size is 1 (react-test-renderer surfaces multiple fiber-tree levels per logical Pressable so a literal `toHaveLength(1)` is too strict — the `Set` of accessibilityLabel values catches the regression where a different element matches the predicate without over-tightening on cardinality). **P4 (MED) NEW source-drift Case 6b** asserts exactly one `<Pressable\b` opening tag in `SkillCard.tsx` via `match(/<Pressable\b/g)` so any future second Pressable trips CI and forces the test author to update Case 6's scope (`extractOpeningTag` returns first match only). **P5 (MED) explicit `jest.mock("expo-secure-store", ...)`** at file level in the runtime smoke test for defense-in-depth — pre-patch the transitive import chain `home/index.tsx` → `useDailyBriefing` → `memory.ts` → `supabase.ts` → `expo-secure-store` relied on jest-expo's auto-mock; a future jest-config change could silently break the chain. **P6 (MED) `beforeEach(() => jest.clearAllMocks())`** added to the runtime smoke test so AsyncStorage / NetInfo / SecureStore / Sentry call history doesn't leak across cases (Story 12-7 / 12-8 precedent). **Additional drift-detector regex tolerance** (triggered by P1/P2): Cases 1 / 3 / 5 / 9 / 10 source-drift regexes + the 2 `extractConstantBody` walker copies loosened to accept the optional `Object.freeze(` wrap — accepts BOTH `= {` (pre-P2) AND `= Object.freeze({` (post-P2) shapes. **+2 net round-1 Jest cases** (1840 → 1842; +16 net since story start vs 1826 baseline). All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 93 suites / 1842 cases). Verified 2026-05-15, story 13-7 (post-review-round-1 patches HIGH × 3 + MED × 3).

**`buildConversationPrompt` perf verification — end-to-end size pinning + Story 11-7 reduction-ratio empirical correction:** post-Epic-13.8, audit "P2-x performance" at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 255](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) closes architecturally **AND Epic 13 is COMPLETE** (8 of 8 stories done; Epic 13 retrospective is the natural next workflow step). Story 11-7 landed the 3 prompt-truncation constants (`MAX_PROMPT_MEMORIES = 3` + `MAX_PROMPT_ERROR_PATTERNS = 3` + `MAX_PROMPT_ITEM_CHARS = 80`) + the `truncateToBytes` pure helper + the sanitize → filter-empty → slice(N) → truncate → filter-empty pipeline — and made 4 perf claims in its CLAUDE.md paragraph that were never empirically verified at the CI layer: (1) "25× reduction on the user-derived tail (~12,000 chars → ~480 chars)"; (2) "~144-288ms TTFT savings per session"; (3) "~$0.001-$0.0018 cost/session at gpt-realtime-mini rates"; (4) "the ~2,500-token base prompt + bilingual prelude + tool-call definitions are unchanged". Existing [`src/lib/prompts/__tests__/conversation-truncation.test.ts`](src/lib/prompts/__tests__/conversation-truncation.test.ts) (27 cases) covered per-block correctness + helper semantics + constant pins but NONE pinned end-to-end prompt size. Story 13-8 lands a **single-axis verification surface** that closes claims #1 + #4 at the CI gate and tracks #2 + #3 as documented operator-action items. **NEW test file at [`src/lib/prompts/__tests__/conversation-prompt-perf.test.ts`](src/lib/prompts/__tests__/conversation-prompt-perf.test.ts)** (~310 lines including JSDoc; 8 logical cases expanded via `it.each` to **17 Jest-reported cases**): Case 1 base prompt size in `[BASE_PROMPT_MIN_CHARS = 3915, BASE_PROMPT_MAX_CHARS = 4184]` (calibrated ±2% from observed B1 base = 4101 chars); Case 2 worst-case prompt size ≤ `WORST_CASE_PROMPT_MAX_CHARS = 7034` (`BASE_PROMPT_MAX_CHARS_PER_MODE + WORST_CASE_TAIL_BUDGET`); Case 3 tail-only bound formula-derived from Story 11-7 constants (`(3 + 3) × (80 + 4) + 1384 = 1888` chars budget; observed 1822 = 3.5% under budget); Case 4 reduction-ratio lower bound `≥ 5×` (observed **6.7×**, not 25× — see below); Case 5 per-CEFR base size invariance across A1–C2 (observed 3.3% spread: A1=3995 / A2=4018 / B1=4101 / B2=4062 / C1=4125 / C2=4053); Case 6 worst-case token-count estimate ≤ `MAX_WORST_CASE_TOKENS = 1759` (observed 1481 tokens for `worst.length = 5923` / 4); Case 7 mode-invariance — `companion=4101 / debate=5045 / tcf_simulation=4811` (observed 23% spread; pinned at `MAX_MODE_SPREAD_RATIO = 0.30` with 7% headroom over current); Case 8 NEGATIVE — `<USER_FACTS>` + `<USER_WEAK_AREAS>` block contents extracted via `extractTagBlockContents` regex; each `"- "` item line in those blocks has content ≤ `MAX_PROMPT_ITEM_CHARS = 80` (defense-in-depth for Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection cap at the post-truncation observability layer; bonus pins `itemLines.length ≤ MAX_PROMPT_MEMORIES / MAX_PROMPT_ERROR_PATTERNS` so the cap-enforcement is also verified at the block-level count). **EMPIRICAL FINDING — Story 11-7's "25× reduction" claim is OVERSTATED at 6.7×.** The discrepancy: Story 11-7 computed 25× against the user-item CONTENT only (`12,000 / ~480 chars` of items); reality includes the `<USER_FACTS>` + `<USER_WEAK_AREAS>` wrapper text (~1,318 chars of bilingual "treat as data" prelude + section-header lines + tag delimiters) which dominates the post-truncation tail. Actual tail = `504 (items) + 1318 (wrapper) = 1822 chars`; reduction = `12,160 / 1822 ≈ 6.7×`. Still a meaningful ~85% reduction in user-derived bytes per session, but the 25× marketing was wrong by ~4×. `MIN_REDUCTION_RATIO = 5` pinned at the CI layer (loose 25% headroom under observed 6.7×) — if a future PR loosens `MAX_PROMPT_ITEM_CHARS` from 80 → 200, the actual tail grows ~40% and the ratio drops to ~4.8× → test fails, alerting the reviewer to the material cost impact. **Cost-per-session reference** (operator-action item; NOT enforced): worst-case 1759 tokens × `cost-table.ts MODEL_RATES["gpt-realtime-mini"]` $10/1M input = $0.0176 (~1.76 cents). At Story 11-4's $1.00/user daily cap, the prompt-input cost is ~1.8% of the cap — negligible. **What 13-8 does NOT do:** no source-code changes outside the test file (`conversation.ts` / `memory.ts` / `realtime-orchestrator.ts` / `cost-table.ts` all zero-diff); no new Sentry breadcrumbs capturing runtime prompt size (future-story extension; would require Story 9-3 telemetry allowlist evaluation); no actual TTFT benchmark (claim #2 stays as operator-documented estimate; would need device profiling out of scope); no cost-table refresh (Story 11-4's quarterly discipline owns rate updates); no new production constants. **Cross-story invariants preserved by construction:** Story 9-3 Sentry allowlist + GDPR scrubber (zero-diff — no telemetry surface) / Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection (Case 8 RE-VERIFIES post-truncation invariant, doesn't relax it) / Story 10-4 vocabulary-tier integration (Case 5's per-CEFR pin captures vocab-tier block-size regressions) / Story 10-7 debate-mode + tcf_simulation (Case 7's mode-invariance check captures mode-block regressions) / Story 11-1 tool-call protocol (orthogonal — tool definitions live in `RealtimeConfig.tools[]`, not in `buildConversationPrompt` output) / Story 11-2 reconnect cached prompt (the cached `systemPrompt` replayed on reconnect IS the output of `buildConversationPrompt`; bounded build-time size = bounded reconnect-replay size) / Story 11-4 daily-cost-cap (Case 6's token-cost reference uses the gpt-realtime-mini rate per cost-table) / Story 11-7 (constants consumed directly by Cases 3 + 4 + 8 via the formula; loosening any constant auto-expands the test budget) / Story 12-1 RealtimeOrchestrator (orthogonal — prompt-building runs upstream) / Story 12-6 transcript cap (orthogonal — separate state) / Story 13-1 through 13-7 (all orthogonal). **0 new packages, 0 migrations, 0 Edge Function changes, 0 CI workflow changes, 0 source-code changes outside the test file** — `package.json` + `package-lock.json` + `supabase/migrations/` + `supabase/functions/` + `.github/workflows/` + `src/lib/prompts/conversation.ts` + `src/lib/memory.ts` + all other production source files zero-diff. **+17 net Jest cases** (1842 → 1859; **exceeds spec target +8 by 9** via `it.each` expansion across the 6 CEFR levels + 3 modes). **Card consolidation — extend SkillCard + introduce ListItemCard; collapse 8 inline card-component declarations into 2 reusable components:** post-Epic-14.2, audit finding **P2-10** (cards portion only — heroes deferred to 14-9) closes architecturally. The pre-14-2 codebase had 9 inline `function Foo(...)` card components scattered across 5 screens with overlapping but inconsistent treatments (different shadow tones, different padding values, different scale-on-press worklets, different left-strip widths). Story 14-2 consolidates them into 2 reusable components per the spec's binding contract: (1) **`src/components/common/SkillCard.tsx` extended** with 3 new props (`featured?: boolean`, `disabled?: boolean`, `accent?: string`) + a SECOND frozen-static-style constant `skillCardFeaturedStaticStyle: ViewStyle = Object.freeze({...}) as ViewStyle` (Story 13-7 R1-P1 `Shadows.card` spread-first + R1-P2 `Object.freeze` mutation defense applied to the new constant; both `@internal` exports for runtime tests). The `featured` variant renders with `Colors.accent10` background + amber border (replaces pre-14-2 inline `VocabularyCard`); the `disabled` variant renders with `opacity: 0.6` + Pressable's `disabled` prop + `accessibilityState={{disabled: true}}` (replaces pre-14-2 inline `ComingSoonCard`); the `accent` prop overrides the left-strip color (defaults to `accentColor`). (2) **NEW `src/components/common/ListItemCard.tsx`** (~210 lines incl. JSDoc) with full slot system: `titlePrimary` (EN per Story 14-1 chrome rule) + `titleSecondary?` (FR pedagogical-reinforcement) + `description?` + `iconEmoji?` + `iconColor?` (tinted icon circle) + `leftStripColor?` (4px-wide accent strip) + `rightContent?` (slot for CEFR badge / count pill / difficulty dots) + `progressBar?` (`{fillPercent, color}` — 2px bar below the title row, clamped 0-100) + `delay?` (entry fade-in cascade) + `onPress?` + `disabled?` + `accessibilityLabel?` + `accessibilityHint?`. When `onPress` is absent the card renders as a static `Animated.View`; when present it wraps in a `Pressable` with scale-on-press worklet + `accessibilityRole="button"`. The `accessibilityLabel` defaults to `${titlePrimary}${description ? \`. ${description}\` : ""}`when not overridden. Frozen-static-style constant`listItemCardStaticStyle`(R1-P1 + P2 patterns). Wrapped in`React.memo`. **8 surface migrations** (1 fewer than the 9-target inventory; `TodayPlanItem` defer documented below): (a) **`app/(tabs)/practice/index.tsx` `VocabularyCard`** (~50 lines deleted) → `<SkillCard ... featured />`. The pre-14-2 `VEDETTE`corner badge was dropped because the`featured` visual treatment (accent10 bg + amber border) IS the featured signal — no separate chrome badge needed (defensible consolidation cost). (b) **`app/(tabs)/mock-test/index.tsx` `SectionCard`** (~80 lines deleted) → `<SkillCard ... />`. Pre-14-2's `nameSub`(EN) primary +`nameFr` (FR) secondary inline render-flip from Story 14-1 R1-H3 is now satisfied via SkillCard's own internal render (titleEn → big text). (c) **`app/(tabs)/mock-test/index.tsx` `ComingSoonCard`** (~40 lines deleted) → `<SkillCard ... disabled />`. The pre-14-2 inline opacity 0.6 + `accessibilityState={{disabled: true}}`+`accessible accessibilityRole="text"`rendering is replaced by SkillCard's disabled variant. The "Coming soon · Epic 10" text is folded into the`description` slot. (d) **`app/(tabs)/profile/index.tsx` `ProfileSkillCard`** (~89 lines deleted) → `<ListItemCard ... progressBar={{fillPercent, color}} rightContent={<CEFRBadgePill level={skillLevel}/>} />`. The CEFR badge pill is extracted as a small co-located helper `CEFRBadgePill`(~12 lines). The pre-14-2 inline FR-primary render (which Story 14-1 R1-H2 had flipped to`.en`) maps directly to `titlePrimary={SKILL*LABELS[skill]?.en ?? skill}`. (e) **`app/(tabs)/profile/index.tsx`error-pattern cards** (~50 lines inline JSX deleted) →`<ListItemCard leftStripColor={Colors.accent} titlePrimary={error.error_description} rightContent={<count-pill JSX>} />`. (f) **`app/(tabs)/conversation/index.tsx` topic cards (`CardItem`)** (~120 lines inline JSX deleted) → `<ListItemCard leftStripColor={LEVEL_COLORS[item.cefr_level]} iconEmoji={TOPIC_EMOJIS[item.titleFr]} iconColor={stripColor} titlePrimary={item.title} titleSecondary={item.titleFr} description={item.description} rightContent={<CEFR badge + difficulty dots stack>} />`. The Story 14-1 chrome rule is preserved by construction: `titlePrimary={item.title}`is EN;`titleSecondary={item.titleFr}` is the French topic name which IS content (the topic the learner discusses). (g) **`src/components/home/TodayPlanItem.tsx`is INTENTIONALLY NOT MIGRATED**. The compact-pill layout (button-radius 12px vs card-radius 16px; tinted skillTint(iconColor, 0.06) background vs surfaceWhite; 28×28 icon circle vs 52×52; minHeight 44 vs ListItemCard's natural ~76) is structurally incompatible with`ListItemCard`'s full-card shape. Forcing the consolidation would visually regress the compact "Today's Plan" rhythm. The defer is captured in the drift detector via a POSITIVE-pin that `TodayPlanItem.tsx`does NOT import`ListItemCard` (so a future half-migration is detected). (h) **`SkillCard.tsx`** (the previously-canonical component) extended with the 3 new props + second frozen constant — Story 13-7 P1 + P2 invariants preserved on both `skillCardPressableStaticStyle`(default) and the new`skillCardFeaturedStaticStyle`. **NEW source-drift detector** at [`src/components/common/**tests**/list-item-card-consolidation-source-drift.test.ts`](src/components/common/__tests__/list-item-card-consolidation-source-drift.test.ts) (12 cases): POSITIVE-pin `listItemCardStaticStyle`exported + frozen +`Shadows.card`spread-FIRST +`@internal`annotated; POSITIVE-pin`SkillCardProps`has all 3 new optional props +`skillCardFeaturedStaticStyle`exported + frozen + uses`Colors.accent10`; NEGATIVE per-screen pin `function VocabularyCard(`/`function SectionCard(`/`function ComingSoonCard(`/`function ProfileSkillCard(`declarations GONE; POSITIVE per-screen pin`<ListItemCard`or`<SkillCard featured/disabled`invocations PRESENT; POSITIVE-pin error-pattern card uses`<ListItemCard leftStripColor={Colors.accent}`; POSITIVE-pin conversation `CardItem`function body renders`<ListItemCard`(not the pre-14-2 bespoke`<TouchableOpacity>...<View className="...mr-3">`block); POSITIVE-pin`TodayPlanItem.tsx`does NOT import`ListItemCard`(defer guard). Uses Story 12-2 P12 comment-stripped`readScreen()` helper + Story 13-7 R1-P4 scoped-element-extraction discipline. **NEW runtime smoke test** at [`src/components/common/**tests**/list-item-card.test.tsx`](src/components/common/__tests__/list-item-card.test.tsx) (9 cases via react-test-renderer + Story 13-7 P3 lessons): Case 1 props rendering (titlePrimary + titleSecondary + description); Case 2 conditional icon circle (only when iconEmoji + iconColor both provided); Case 3 left strip render-condition; Case 4 rightContent slot verbatim; Case 5 progressBar fill percent + color; Case 6a onPress fires when not disabled; Case 6b onPress is no-op when disabled + accessibilityState propagates; Case 7 accessibilityLabel default vs override; Case 8 `listItemCardStaticStyle`is`Object.freeze`'d (Story 13-7 R1-P2 mutation defense pin). Mocks `react-native-reanimated`via the shared`src/test-utils/mocks/reanimated.ts`factory (Epic 13 retro AI #7); uses the shared`MinimalTestInstance`+`findAllNodes`+`flattenStyle`helpers from`src/test-utils/react-test-renderer.ts`. **Cross-story invariants preserved by construction:** Story 9-3 Sentry allowlist zero-diff (no telemetry surface) / Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection N/A (no AI / no prompts) / Story 11-1 tool-call protocol N/A / Story 11-2 reconnect + barge-in N/A / Story 12-1 RealtimeOrchestrator orthogonal / Story 12-6 transcript cap orthogonal (no transcript surface) / Story 13-1 transcript render-storm fix orthogonal (TranscriptView untouched) / Story 13-7 frozen-static-style pattern preserved across all 3 components (`skillCardPressableStaticStyle`unchanged, NEW`skillCardFeaturedStaticStyle`follows the same R1-P1 + P2 patterns, NEW`listItemCardStaticStyle`does too) / Story 14-1 chrome rule preserved (consumers pass`SKILL_LABELS[skill]?.en`to`titlePrimary`; `titleFr`/`nameFr`go to`titleSecondary`as pedagogical-reinforcement secondary line; never primary chrome). **Net diff: +469 LOC added (mostly tests + ListItemCard) − 372 LOC deleted (inline component declarations) = net +97 LOC** (slightly positive vs the spec's "net negative ~400-500 LOC" estimate; the variance comes from the runtime smoke test being heavier than estimated + the SkillCard extensions also adding a non-trivial second frozen constant + new prop wiring; the consolidation goal — fewer inline component declarations, single source of truth for card visual treatment — is met regardless of the LOC delta sign). **0 new packages, 0 migrations, 0 Edge Function changes, 0 CI workflow changes** — load-bearing scope discipline (4 source files modified + 2 new test files + 1 new component + 4 housekeeping files = 11 files total; ~700 lines diff). The`TouchableOpacity`import in`conversation/index.tsx`is retained because other untouched JSX in the same file still uses it (the conversation-mode pills + the hero avatar pill at lines 247 / 279 / 304); the`Story 14-1 R1`chrome rule applies but`TouchableOpacity`is not chrome. The`Mon profil`Story 14-1 R1 miss at`profile/index.tsx:163`is a pre-existing chrome-rule gap not addressed in 14-2 scope — flagged for`chore/14-1-followup`backlog. **Drift-test ripple** — Story 14-1's`language-strategy-source-drift.test.ts` had 3 assertions that referenced pre-14-2 inline component structures (`VEDETTE`badge presence,`font-bold text-primary">{nameSub}`mock-test render-flip pin, bare`Vocabulaire`global-sweep substring). Updated each to reflect the post-14-2 SkillCard consolidation: VEDETTE badge assertion dropped (replaced with`titleEn="Vocabulary"`invocation pin); mock-test render-flip pin updated to verify`<SkillCard\b`invocation +`titleEn={section.nameSub}`consumer wiring; bare`Vocabulaire`global-sweep substring anchored to`>Vocabulaire<`(chrome-context) so it doesn't false-flag the`titleFr="Vocabulaire"`prop value (which is FR content per Story 14-1 chrome rule, not chrome). Story 13-7's`animated-wrapper-className-style-source-drift.test.ts`Case 6 (inner Pressable style-prop assertion) updated to accept BOTH the pre-14-2 literal`style={skillCardPressableStaticStyle}`AND the post-14-2`style={[containerStyle, disabled ? ... : null]}`array form (the new`containerStyle`local routes between the 2 frozen variants). Verified 2026-05-15, story 14-2. **Story 14-2 review-round-1 patches** (HIGH × 4 + MED × 7 = 11 patches; ~10 deferred; ~3 rejected as noise): adversarial 3-layer review (Blind Hunter 18 + Edge Case Hunter 18 + Acceptance Auditor verdict **APPROVE_WITH_NOTES** 13 LOW/INFO) converged on **a11y regressions on the consolidated disabled state + drift-detector hardening + a Story 14-1 R1 chrome miss the consolidation touched but didn't fix**. **H1** — disabled SkillCard a11y regression: pre-14-2 inline ComingSoonCard used`accessibilityRole="text"`+`accessibilityHint="Not yet available"`for the Writing "Coming soon" entry. Post-14-2 the consolidated`SkillCard.disabled`branch was rendering`accessibilityRole="button"`+`accessibilityHint="Double tap to start Writing practice"`— VoiceOver/TalkBack would tell users to interact with a non-interactive card. Fixed via conditional`accessibilityRole={disabled ? "text" : "button"}`+`accessibilityHint={disabled ? "Not yet available" : "Double tap to start ${titleEn} practice"}`. **H2** — `ListItemCard.progressBar.fillPercent = NaN`breaks RN layout:`Math.max(0, Math.min(100, NaN))`returns NaN →`width: "NaN%"`which RN treats as undefined. Trigger: a consumer passing`undefined / 7`. Fixed with `Number.isFinite`guard. **H3** — Case 6b runtime test vacuously passes:`pressFn = pressables[0].props.onPress`is`undefined`when disabled, then`if (typeof pressFn === "function") pressFn()`short-circuits. Fixed — now also asserts`disabled`prop literally true,`onPress`literally undefined, and exercises`onPressIn`+`onPressOut`(each has its own`disabled`guard). **H4** —`ListItemCard`non-press branch missing`accessibilityRole`: pre-14-2 inline static cards had `accessible accessibilityRole="text"`; Android TalkBack would skip focus or read only the first child Text. Fixed — non-press branch now sets `accessible accessibilityRole="text"`+ wires`accessibilityHint`through (L1 fold-in: was silently dropped). **M1** — Writing card cascade-timing regression: pre-R1 14-2 set`delay={0}`while Listening/Reading cascade was still animating. Fixed — Writing`delay={SECTIONS.length * 80}`+ Speaking pushed to`(SECTIONS.length + 1) _ 80`. **M3** — drift detector scope-leakage: `/<SkillCard[\s\S]_?disabled/` could false-pass on sibling element pair. Tightened via count-based sibling defense (`allSkillCards.length >= 2`AND`disabled`substring present). **M4 + M5** —`skillCardFeaturedStaticStyle`drift gaps: pre-R1 only`listItemCardStaticStyle`had`Shadows.card`spread-first +`@internal`pins. Added pins for the second frozen constant via`indexOf`ordering check + RAW-source`@internal[\s\S]_?skillCardFeaturedStaticStyle`regex. **M6** —`TodayPlanItem`defer pin only caught`@/`alias path; tightened to bare token match`\bListItemCard\b`so relative-path or barrel-export half-migrations also fail. **M7** —`COMMENT_STRIP_RE`extended to JSX comments via`\{\s*\/\*[^{}]*?\*\/\s*\}`alternation FIRST. **Load-bearing** subtlety: the`[^{}]*?`brace-exclusion (NOT`[\s\S]_?`) — without it the regex over-matches TypeScript `interface { /\*\* field \_/ ... }`bodies, verified empirically when the pre-patch version chewed through`TodayPlanItem.tsx`'s interface body and broke the positive `React.memo`pin. **M10** —`Mon profil`Story 14-1 R1 miss at`profile/index.tsx:163`was flagged-for-followup pre-R1. Acceptance Auditor + Edge Case Hunter both flagged that 14-2 already touched the file — fix is free. Converted to`My profile`. **M11** — Story 13-7 drift Case 6 hybrid-regression door: post-14-2 Case 6 accepted BOTH `style={skillCardPressableStaticStyle}`AND`style={[containerStyle, ...]}`. A future refactor writing `style={[skillCardPressableStaticStyle, animStyle]}`(the OLD constant directly inside an array, bypassing the`containerStyle`indirection) would have passed the alternation's first arm vacuously. Added negative-guard for both static-style constants. **M13** — ProfileSkillCard progress bar width regression: pre-14-2 the bar was full-card-width; post-14-2 it was squeezed inside`<View style={{flex:1}}>`so a 75% fill visually represented ~50% of card width. Fixed — split rendering: when`progressBar !== undefined`, content-row + progress-row stack vertically inside a `flex:1`wrapper so the bar spans full card width below the title row. **+1 net round-1 Jest case** (1916 → 1917; the other patches tightened existing assertions in place). All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 97 suites / 1917 cases). **~10 findings deferred** (icon-circle tint 12.5% → 9% — defensible consolidation cost; unused imports false alarms;`featured + disabled`undefined behavior — no current caller; dead code branches; cosmetic helper wrap; Story 14-1 multi-line`>Vocabulaire<`tolerance — per-file POSITIVE pin already covers; promote`getAllTextContent`to shared utils — future refactor). **~3 findings rejected as noise** (Acceptance Auditor's`SkillCard.accent`unused — authorized forward-compat scaffolding per AC #2; AC #9 text-vs-impl`CardItem` drift — impl is correct, AC text is documentation drift; TodayPlanItem defer well-documented per Story 13-4 R1 noise-reduction). **Audit P2-10 cards portion still architecturally met** — the a11y regressions on the disabled SkillCard branch + the progress-bar width regression on ListItemCard would have visibly broken the "single source of truth" goal at the user-facing layer; now closed. Heroes portion still deferred to Story 14-9. Verified 2026-05-16, story 14-2 (post-review-round-1 patches HIGH × 4 + MED × 7).

**Icon system replacement — NEW `src/components/common/Icon.tsx` wraps `@expo/vector-icons.Feather` + 33 emoji-to-icon migrations:** post-Epic-14.3, audit roadmap line 272 (icon system replacement) closes architecturally. Pre-14-3 the codebase rendered ~35 emoji occurrences across 16 source files as if they were chrome icons (Mail input affordance, Mic CTA, Headphones skill card, etc). Emoji-as-icon is OS-inconsistent (the same `🎤` glyph renders as a studio microphone on iOS and a generic mic on Android), scales unpredictably under accessibility-scale, and surfaces poor screen-reader semantics ("envelope, U+2709" instead of "Email input"). Story 14-3 lands a **single-source-of-truth icon wrapper** + **33 emoji → Feather migrations** while preserving 12 conversation-topic emoji + 6 onboarding-goal emoji as LEARNING CONTENT (Story 14-1 chrome/content rule). **(1) NEW [`src/components/common/Icon.tsx`](src/components/common/Icon.tsx)** (~90 lines incl. JSDoc) wraps `@expo/vector-icons.Feather` (already transitive via Expo SDK 55 — zero install cost; verified `@expo/vector-icons@15.1.1` in `node_modules/`). Exports `Icon` (React.memo'd; consistent with `SkillCard` / `ListItemCard` / `Bubble` precedents) + `IconProps` + `IconName` typed union with 22 members (`mail` / `lock` / `user` / `mic` / `headphones` / `book-open` / `edit-3` / `activity` / `volume-2` / `file-text` / `repeat` / `globe` / `book` / `check` / `check-circle` / `key` / `zap` / `target` / `message-circle` / `award` / `smile` / `settings`). The typed union is **compile-time gate against icon-name typos** — `<Icon name="mial" />` fails `tsc` (where `<Feather name="mial" />` would silently render a missing-glyph placeholder at runtime). Defaults: `size = 24`, `color = Colors.textPrimary`. **Accessibility default** (Story 14-2 R1-H1 a11y-regression lesson applied) — when `accessibilityLabel` is omitted, sets `importantForAccessibility="no"` so screen-readers treat the icon as decorative-of-text (an enclosing `<TextInput accessibilityLabel="Email address" />` already owns the announcement). Consumers that need the icon announced as its own element pass `accessibilityLabel` explicitly. **(2) Extended `SkillCard` + `ListItemCard` with `iconNode?: React.ReactNode` slot** — when provided, renders this React node inside the existing icon-circle in place of the `iconEmoji` `<Text>` element. Consumers pass `<Icon name="headphones" />` JSX directly. The legacy `iconEmoji` prop stays required on `SkillCard` (the 12 conversation topic cards still pass `TOPIC_EMOJIS[...]` as content); the `iconNode` slot OVERRIDES the rendered child when present. Same pattern on `ListItemCard` (where `iconEmoji` was already optional). **(3) Extended `TodayPlanItem` with `iconName?: IconName` prop** — when provided, renders via `<Icon />` instead of the `iconEmoji` `<Text>`. The `iconName` takes precedence over `iconEmoji`; the legacy emoji prop is preserved for future content-emoji surfaces. The Story 14-2 defer rationale (compact-pill layout incompatible with `ListItemCard`'s full-card geometry) is unchanged — Story 14-3 extends TodayPlanItem with an icon prop, NOT a consolidation. **(4) `use-daily-briefing.ts` `TodayPlanItem` shape** — `iconEmoji: string` field DELETED ("delete don't alias" pattern); replaced with `iconName: IconName`. All 4 plan-item builder paths (SRS due / error pattern / weakest skill / fallback conversation) emit typed `IconName` values; the per-skill emoji map (5 entries) is replaced with a per-skill `IconName` map (`listening: "headphones"` / `reading: "book-open"` / `writing: "edit-3"` / `speaking: "message-circle"` / `grammar: "file-text"`). Home screen consumer at `app/(tabs)/home/index.tsx` passes `iconName={item.iconName}` to TodayPlanItem (was `iconEmoji={item.iconEmoji}`). **(5) 33 chrome / status / decoration emoji REPLACED** across 11 source files: **CHROME (8)** — `login.tsx` mail + lock; `signup.tsx` user + mail + lock; `forgot-password.tsx` mail; `home/index.tsx` ConversationCard mic; `conversation/index.tsx` CONVERSATION_MODES `💬` companion-mode icon (refactored to discriminated-union `{kind: "icon", name: "message-circle"} | {kind: "emoji", value: string}` so debate `⚔️` + tcf_sim `🎯` stay as decorative emoji since Feather lacks crossed-swords/target-bullseye for those semantic positions). **SKILL/SECTION (16)** — `mock-test/index.tsx` SECTIONS listening + reading; mock-test Writing + Speaking production cards; `mock-test/results.tsx` SECTION_LABELS 3 entries (listening/reading/grammar legacy); `practice/index.tsx` PRACTICE_SKILLS 8 entries refactored from `emoji: string` to `iconName: IconName`; `practice/index.tsx` Vocabulary featured card; `practice/vocabulary.tsx` hero; `use-daily-briefing.ts` 4 surfaces (SRS / error / weakest-skill map / fallback). **STATUS (4)** — `vocabulary.tsx` `🎉` celebration → `award` + `✅` caught-up → `check-circle`; `[sessionId].tsx` strengths `✓` → `check`; `PasswordStrengthIndicator.tsx` checklist `✓` met state → `check` (unmet `·` bullet preserved as text — not an emoji). **DECORATION (2 per operator decisions)** — Q3 `profile/index.tsx` streak `🔥` → `Icon name="zap"` (Feather lacks Flame; visual semantic shift warmth → energy documented for operator; the FR "jour/jours" streak label is preserved as pre-existing content); Q4 `forgot-password.tsx` hero `🔑` 52px → `Icon name="key"` 52px (auth-surface consistency with the mail input icon below). **(6) 18 LEARNING CONTENT emoji PRESERVED** — `conversation/index.tsx` `TOPIC_EMOJIS` constant (12 entries: `👋 ☕ 🗺️ 👨‍👩‍👧 🏥 📅 💼 ✈️ 📰 🎬 🍷 🧠`) — these are the topics the learner discusses in French; the emoji visually anchors the topic. `onboarding/index.tsx` goal-selection emoji (6 entries) per Q2 recommended (content side of chrome/content split). `use-session-feedback-aggregate.ts` milestone celebration emoji (`🏆 🎯`) — decorative celebration glyphs, not chrome affordances; not in inventory. The drift detector's POSITIVE-pin against `TOPIC_EMOJIS` declaration is the load-bearing guard against future "let's clean up all emoji" passes that would erode the content boundary. **5 operator-decision items resolved per spec recommendations:** Q1 icon library → `@expo/vector-icons.Feather` (already transitive — zero install cost; All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 99 suites / 1940 cases). Verified 2026-05-16, story 14-3. **Story 14-3 review-round-1 patches** (HIGH × 3 + MED × 3 = 6 patches; 4 deferred; ~10 rejected as noise): adversarial 3-layer review (Blind Hunter 11 findings + Edge Case Hunter 17 findings + Acceptance Auditor verdict **APPROVE_WITH_NOTES** 4 LOW/INFO) converged on **iOS a11y regression on Icon decorative default + drift-detector completeness gaps + a TodayPlanItem lying-contract**. **P1 (HIGH) — iOS a11y regression**: pre-R1 Icon decorative default only set `importantForAccessibility="no"` which is **Android-only in React Native**; on iOS it's a no-op so VoiceOver still focused the icon beside labeled `TextInput`s (auth-surface mail/lock/user icons announced as "Mail, image" beside the Email input that already had its own label). Post-patch the decorative branch sets THREE props for cross-platform parity: `accessible={false}` (iOS canonical decorative flag) + `accessibilityElementsHidden={true}` (iOS-strong hide; VoiceOver tree-walker skips this node + descendants) + `importantForAccessibility="no"` (Android canonical). Mirrors Story 14-2 `PasswordStrengthIndicator.tsx:152-156` pattern. Runtime test Case 5 strengthened to pin all 3 flags; new Case 6 verifies that when `accessibilityLabel` IS provided, the decorative flags are NOT set (consumer-controlled announcement preserved). **P2 (HIGH) — `TodayPlanItem` lying-contract**: pre-R1 the `iconName?` + `iconEmoji?` props were both-optional with a JSDoc-only invariant "one of the two MUST be provided"; the render block's `iconEmoji ?? ""` fallback would silently produce an empty 28×28 tinted circle when both props were missing. Post-patch a 3-arm conditional renders `<Icon>` when `iconName` provided, then `<Text>{iconEmoji}</Text>` when emoji provided, else a question-mark placeholder (textTertiary color) — visible signal that surfaces the gap instead of an invisible empty circle. JSDoc tightened to document the runtime-fallback contract. **P3 (HIGH) — drift detector NEGATIVE-pin completeness**: pre-R1 the `use-daily-briefing.ts` drift case had NEGATIVE pins for only 2 of 5 legacy `iconEmoji` literals (📚 + 🎯); the per-skill `emojiMap: Record<TCFSkill, string>` (🎧 📖 ✍️ 💬 📝) was entirely unguarded against regression. TypeScript catches re-introduction at the field-type level (`iconName: IconName` on TodayPlanItem interface), but belt-and-suspenders POSITIVE+NEGATIVE pin discipline (Story 13-2 P11 lesson) was incomplete. Same gap existed in the `signup.tsx` drift case (✉️ + 🔒 missing from negative pins; only 👤 covered). Post-patch BOTH drift cases enumerate ALL legacy emoji as negative pins. **P4 (MED) — `PasswordStrengthIndicator` vertical-jitter**: the new `<View width={14}>` wrapper had NO explicit `height`; the Icon path (12pt-tall glyph) and the `·` Text path (caption line-height ~16-18pt) would jiggle the checklist row height on every keystroke as requirements toggled met/unmet. Post-patch added `height: 18` so both child paths render in the same fixed vertical slot regardless of which child renders. **P5 (MED) — `TodayPlanItem` icon contrast**: Edge Case Hunter found that rendering the icon at full `color={iconColor}` saturation inside a `backgroundColor: skillTint(iconColor, 0.12)` circle reduces WCAG AA contrast on light-tint skill colors (vocabulary amber, listening blue) — monochrome icon at 100% saturation of the SAME hue as its 12% tint background washes out. Post-patch the Icon foreground uses `Colors.textPrimary` (navy `#1E3A5F`) which gives high contrast on every `skillTint` background; the `iconColor` still anchors the circle tint as before. **P6 (MED) — `home/index.tsx` raw-glyph drift pin**: pre-R1 the negative pin targeted only the JS escape-sequence form `\\uD83C\\uDF99\\uFE0F`; a future code-format pass that converted to literal 4-byte UTF-8 `🎙️` while keeping the Icon would silently pass. Post-patch pins both the escape form AND the raw-glyph form. **Plus 3 LOW polish**: (a) TOPIC_EMOJIS drift regex made format-tolerant (accepts EITHER `\\u00e9` escape form OR literal `é` — defensive against future Prettier auto-format passes); (b) Completion Notes Q5 wording corrected from "3 sites" → "2 sites" (mock-test/index.tsx no longer has a Grammar section per TCF Canada spec; the spec inventory had pre-existing factual drift); (c) CLAUDE.md file count corrected from "17 files total" → "22 files total" (3 new + 16 source + 3 housekeeping). **Deferred (4)**: SkillCard.emoji-required-while-callers-pass-empty-string API smell (cosmetic; defensible per Story 14-2 forward-compat scaffolding precedent); IconName maintenance burden documentation (future operator concern); conversation-mode pill active-state visual asymmetry (Icon vs emoji — defensible per Q1 trade-off; debate/tcf_sim arms keep emoji because Feather lacks crossed-swords/target-bullseye semantic icons); sessionId Strengths/Improvements `→` arrow asymmetry (not in 14-3 inventory; filed for `chore/14-3-followup`). **Rejected as noise (10+)**: AC #4 "16" inventory drift (pre-existing spec count, not impl); AC #11 Q5 "3 sites" (corrected in P-LOW); Acceptance Auditor's 4 LOW/INFO bookkeeping items below blocking threshold; `findFeatherProps` predicate non-uniqueness (matches today's mock correctly; future test-infra concern); Mock leaks name into Text children (Jest-only artifact; no test pollution today); React.memo over-rerendering (self-withdrawn by Blind Hunter); 18px Icon visual size shift (defensible per operator framing); IconName union member-count regex strictness (vacuous self-withdraw); `mock-test/results.tsx` legacy-section blank rendering (pre-existing; 14-3 doesn't worsen). **+5 net round-1 Jest cases** (1940 → 1941; impl: new Case 6 in icon.test.tsx — the other patches tightened existing assertions in place). All 4 quality gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / jest 99 suites / 1941 cases). Audit roadmap line 272 still architecturally met — the iOS a11y regression on the Icon decorative default would have visibly broken the "icon system" goal on iOS VoiceOver users; now closed. **CI coverage gating — `jest --coverage` wired into CI with 40% threshold floor on `src/lib/` + `src/hooks/`:** post-Epic-15.6, the SIXTH and final Epic 15 (Test Coverage & QA Infrastructure) story closes the Epic 15.6 deliverable at [`shippable-roadmap.md` line 299](_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/shippable-roadmap.md) ("CI gating — Jest threshold ≥ 40% on `src/lib/` and `src/hooks/`; fail PR on regression."). Pre-15-6 the repo had **2167+ Jest tests across libs / hooks / components / prompts / schemas** (the Story 12-10 audit-refresh footnote corrected the pre-15-X audit's stale "3-5% coverage" framing) but **no CI coverage gate** — a PR that removed tests or added substantial untested code merged silently. Story 15-6 lands the gate. **(1) [`jest.config.js`](jest.config.js)** extended with three additive blocks: `collectCoverageFrom: ["src/lib/**/*.{ts,tsx}", "src/hooks/**/*.{ts,tsx}", "!**/__tests__/**", "!**/*.d.ts"]` (scope matches spec deliverable), `coverageThreshold: { global: { statements: 40, branches: 40, functions: 40, lines: 40 } }` (40% floor per spec literal — the audit's `≥ 40%` mandate is the starting bar, not the aspirational ceiling), and `coverageReporters: ["text-summary", "lcov"]` (text-summary for CI log readability; lcov for future Codecov / Coveralls integration without re-running). **(2) [`package.json`](package.json)** gains a new `test:coverage` script wired to `jest --coverage` (placed adjacent to `test:watch` for adjacency). **(3) [`.github/workflows/ci.yml`](.github/workflows/ci.yml)** gains a new step `Tests with coverage threshold` running `npm run test:coverage` IMMEDIATELY AFTER the existing `Tests` step (Q1 RECOMMENDED — keep both for separation of concerns: fast green-light feedback before the slower instrumented run). The new step does NOT carry `continue-on-error: true` (Story 12-10 R1-H2 silent-disable defense) and does NOT carry an `if:` key (defense-in-depth against accidental gate-skipping). **(4) Measured coverage baseline at gate introduction (2026-05-17)**: Statements **53.42%** (2325/4352) / Branches **55.80%** (1417/2539) / Functions **51.49%** (362/703) / Lines **54.12%** (2126/3928). The 40% spec floor leaves **≈11 points of headroom against the lowest metric (Functions)** — sufficient for a future PR to add untested code without breaking CI immediately, while a sustained regression (e.g., a deleted test file dropping Functions below 40%) trips the gate. Q2 RECOMMENDED was "measured floor minus 3%" but the 40% spec literal already leaves comfortable headroom, so the spec floor was used as-is. A future PR can ratchet to 50% once Functions coverage grows (filed as `15-6-followup-coverage-ratchet-cadence`). **(5) NEW drift detector** at [`src/lib/__tests__/ci-coverage-gate-source-drift.test.ts`](src/lib/__tests__/ci-coverage-gate-source-drift.test.ts) (6 cases via Story 12-2 P12 source-string drift pattern + Story 13-2 P11 paired POSITIVE+NEGATIVE pin discipline + Story 12-10 R1-M1 indexOf-ordering anchor + Story 12-10 R1-H2 step-block-scoped negative guard): (a) `coverageThreshold` whole-block regex with 40 floor on all 4 metrics (single-regex pin catches partial-drop e.g., dropping `branches`), (b) `collectCoverageFrom` 4-entry per-key pins (`src/lib/**/*.{ts,tsx}` + `src/hooks/**/*.{ts,tsx}` + `!**/__tests__/**` + `!**/*.d.ts`), (c) `package.json` `test:coverage` script value === `"jest --coverage"` exactly, (d) `ci.yml` step name + `npm run test:coverage` run command, (e) `coverageStepIdx > testsStepIdx` ordering (Story 12-10 R1-M1 anchor-on-exact-step-name pattern), (f) NEGATIVE within the coverage step's block: no `continue-on-error: true` and no `if:` (Story 12-10 R1-H2 lesson — scope the silent-disable check to the step block, not the file). **(6) `coverage/` directory** added to both `.gitignore` and `.prettierignore` so the generated lcov + HTML report don't get tracked or reformatted. **3 operator decisions resolved per Recommended**: Q1 keep both `Tests` + `Tests with coverage threshold` steps (fast feedback + slow gate); Q2 use spec-literal 40% (vs measured-floor-minus-3% — spec floor already leaves ≈11 points of headroom); Q3 defer Codecov / Coveralls integration to operator-action follow-up `15-6-followup-codecov-integration` (needs Codecov account setup). **Closes Epic 15.6 deliverable architecturally** + closes the audit-mandated "CI must be a real gate, not green-light theater" framing (Story 12-10's `--audit-level=high` audit gate + Story 15-6's `--coverage` threshold gate together form the two-layer CI quality bar — vulns + tests). **Cross-story invariants preserved by construction:** Story 9-3 Sentry allowlist zero-diff (no telemetry surface — coverage is a build-time metric) / Story 9-4 stored-prompt-injection N/A / Story 11-X / 12-X / 13-X / 14-X / 15-1 through 15-5 all orthogonal (the coverage gate runs the existing suite + measures it; doesn't modify any source surface). **0 source-module modifications** beyond the 5 spec-allowed surfaces (`jest.config.js`, `package.json`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml`, `.gitignore`, `.prettierignore`) + 1 new drift test + 1 spec/sprint-status/CLAUDE.md trio. **Regression-tested with +6 net Jest cases** (2159 → 2165; matches spec target +5–7 squarely in range). All 5 design-system gates green (type-check 0 errors / lint 0 warnings / prettier clean / check:tokens clean / jest 116 suites / 2165 tests / coverage gate passes by ≈11 points on each metric). **Epic 15 implementation work is COMPLETE — 6 of 6 stories done; Epic 15 retrospective is the natural next workflow step.** Verified 2026-05-17, story 15-6.

**Conversation Buddy 2.0 — persona + conversation-driver + comprehension-support prompt blocks + silence relance:** post-Epic-18.1 (v2-vision-roadmap Epic 18; first v2 story), the conversation experience becomes the "close pal who happens to be a tutor" the product vision targets. **Prompt side** (`src/lib/prompts/conversation.ts`): close-pal Role bullet (all modes) + `## Driving the Conversation` block (AI must end every turn with a question/invitation; follows short answers with easier related questions; steers toward remembered user facts; primed for `[SYSTEM NUDGE]` items) + `## Comprehension Support` block (level-adaptive English: A1-A2 proactive one-line clarifications + glosses via shared `BEGINNER_COMPREHENSION_SUPPORT` const; B1 English-as-fallback; B2+ French-only — band-shared strings hoisted to consts per review R1 so twins can't drift). Both blocks gated by NEW exported `modeSupportsConversationDriving(mode)` — the single source of truth consumed by BOTH the prompt builder AND the orchestrator's relance gate (tcf_simulation excluded per Story 10-6 prep-window contract; exam mode also keeps the strict "ONLY in French" Role rule while driving-enabled modes get a deferential rule that defers to Comprehension Support — review R1 contradiction fix). NEW exported `RELANCE_NUDGE_TEXT` lives in the prompt module (single source with the runtime nudge). **Orchestrator side** (`src/lib/realtime-orchestrator.ts`): silence relance — `RELANCE_DELAY_MS = 15_000` timer armed on `response.done`, fires a system-role `conversation.item.create` (client-generated id) + `response.create` (item-injection preserves the session prompt; `response.instructions` would replace it). Review-round-1 hardening (HIGH × 8 from 8-angle adversarial review): (1) counter resets ONLY on a COMMITTED user turn (created user item with non-empty transcript, or `sendText`) — NOT raw VAD `speech_started` (ambient-noise blips would re-open the budget → unbounded chain ≈ $5-25/hr unmetered); (2) `MAX_RELANCES_PER_SESSION = 4` hard lifetime cap, never resets mid-session — the load-bearing economic bound since relance `response.create` is client-initiated spend the Story 11-4 mid-session ledger does not meter; (3) arm-time + fire-time `state.isSpeaking` guards (a barge-in's cancelled response emits a terminal `response.done` AFTER `speech_started` cleared the timer — without the guard the relance would nudge a slow learner mid-sentence); (4) `AppState.currentState !== "active"` fire guard (no paid unhearable audio from a backgrounded/locked phone); (5) `sendText` clears the timer + restores the budget (text users are engaged users); (6) `realtime.reconnected` re-arms explicitly (fresh server context per Story 11-2 produces no `response.done` without user action); (7) counters increment ONLY on a delivered send (`isConnected` checked inside `safeSessionCall` — null-session / not-OPEN drops don't burn the budget); (8) the nudge item is DELETED from server context once served (`response.done`) or stale (race) via `cleanupRelanceItem` so a "[SYSTEM NUDGE] user has been quiet" instruction can never linger and color later turns. `conversation_already_has_active_response` is benign ONLY within `RELANCE_RACE_WINDOW_MS = 5_000` of a delivered relance (scoped in `handleErrorEvent` BEFORE the global `isBenignBargeInRace` check — a global suppression would mute the one error exposing future double-`response.create` bugs; outside the window it routes to `captureError` as before). Sentry: 1 new `feature` tag `realtime-relance` + breadcrumb keys `attempt`/`total` (small integers; Story 9-3 allowlist conventions). Prompt-size budgets deliberately recalibrated (+~1,200 chars ≈ ~300 tokens ≈ +$0.003/session at gpt-realtime-mini — accepted buddy-behavior cost; see Numerical Claims Index 18-1 rows); Story 11-7 tail constants + reduction-ratio pins UNCHANGED. Deferred from review: shared orchestrator-test mock-harness extraction to `src/test-utils/mocks/` (6th copy shipped; Epic 13 retro AI #7 pattern) + typed `RealtimeSession.sendSystemMessage` envelope helper + relance-count persistence for future ledger metering. Regression-tested in `src/lib/__tests__/realtime-orchestrator-relance.test.ts` (21 behavioral cases incl. ambient-noise-no-reset + lifetime-cap + mid-speech guards + backgrounded + undelivered-send + scoped-race-window + reconnect-re-arm + nudge-item cleanup) + `conversation.test.ts` Story 18-1 describe block (6 content pins: block presence in companion/debate + absence in tcf_simulation + French-rule variants + gate helper truth table + nudge-text export). Verified 2026-07-18, story 18-1 (post-review-round-1 patches HIGH × 8 + doc/test hygiene).

### Routing (`app/`)

Expo Router file-based routing with three route groups:

- `(auth)/` — login, signup, forgot-password (unauthenticated)
- `onboarding/` — post-signup 3-step wizard
- `(tabs)/` — main app with 5 tabs: home, conversation, practice, mock-test, profile

Auth guard in `app/_layout.tsx` redirects based on session state and onboarding status.

### Application Logic (`src/`)

- **`src/hooks/`** — Custom hooks that are the primary interface for features. Each hook manages its own Supabase queries and API calls:
- `use-auth.ts` — sign in/up/out, profile loading, onAuthStateChange subscription
- `use-realtime-voice.ts` — orchestrates OpenAI Realtime WebSocket voice conversations
- `use-exercise.ts` — AI exercise generation and grading via GPT-4o
- `use-pronunciation.ts` — Azure Speech pronunciation assessment
- `use-progress.ts` — skill progress and streaks from Supabase
- `use-audio-recorder.ts` / `use-audio-player.ts` — expo-av recording/playback

- **`src/lib/`** — Core libraries and API clients:
- `openai.ts` — OpenAI client (chat completions, TTS, embeddings) via `ai-proxy` Edge Function
- `realtime.ts` — `RealtimeSession` class managing WebSocket to OpenAI Realtime API via `realtime-session` Edge Function
- `supabase.ts` — Supabase client with expo-secure-store adapter for native sessions
- `pronunciation.ts` — Azure Speech pronunciation assessment via `pronunciation-assess` Edge Function
- `scoring.ts` — TCF score math (raw% → TCF scale, CEFR mapping)
- `srs.ts` — SM-2 spaced repetition algorithm for vocabulary
- `memory.ts` — Vector-based companion memory (extract facts, embed, store, retrieve via pgvector)
- `error-tracker.ts` — recurring error pattern tracking and micro-drill generation
- `prompts/` — System prompt builders per feature (conversation, grammar, listening, reading, writing, mock-test)

- **`src/store/`** — Zustand stores:
- `auth-store.ts` — session, user, profile, isOnboarded

- **`src/types/`** — TypeScript types for CEFR/TCF domain, conversations, exercises, user profile

- **`src/components/`** — Reusable UI components organized by feature (conversation/, practice/)

### Database (`supabase/migrations/`)

- `001_initial_schema.sql` — All tables, RLS policies, auth trigger
- `002_memory_functions.sql` — `match_memories()` pgvector RPC function

Tables include: profiles, skill_progress, conversations, conversation_messages, exercises, vocabulary, mock_tests, mock_test_answers, daily_activity, companion_memory, error_patterns. All have RLS enforcing `auth.uid() = user_id`.

### Styling

NativeWind v4 (Tailwind for React Native). Custom theme in `tailwind.config.js`:

- `primary`: navy blue (`#1E3A5F`)
- `accent`: amber/gold (`#F5A623`)
- `success`: `#34C759`, `error`: `#FF3B30`
- `surface`: off-white (`#F5F5F0`)

Global CSS at `src/styles/global.css`.

## Key Conventions

- **Path alias**: `@/*` maps to repo root (e.g., `import { supabase } from '@/src/lib/supabase'`)
- **TypeScript strict mode** enabled
- **Typed routes** enabled (`experiments.typedRoutes` in app.json)
- All AI API calls are proxied through Supabase Edge Functions (`ai-proxy`, `realtime-session`, `pronunciation-assess`) — API keys never leave the server
- All Supabase tables use Row-Level Security scoped to `auth.uid()`
- The `components/` directory at repo root contains unused Expo boilerplate — new components go in `src/components/`
